<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>I was a very small boy when I received the bite. My parents tried everything, but in those days there was no cure. The potion that Professor Snape has been making for me is a very recent discovery. It makes me safe, you see. As long as I take it in the week, preceding the keep my mind when I transform... I’m able to curl up in my office, a harmless <a href="/wiki/Wolf" title="Wolf">wolf</a>, and wait for the moon to wane again. Before the <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a> was discovered, however, I became a fully fledged monster once a month. It seemed impossible that I would be able to come to Hogwarts. Other parents weren’t likely to want their children exposed to me. </i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin's life as a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">Werewolf</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><b>Professor Remus John</b><sup id="cite_ref-WBD_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WBD-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> <b>Lupin</b>, <span class="template-c"><a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">O.M. (First Class)</a></span>, (<a href="/wiki/10_March" title="10 March">10 March</a>, <a href="/wiki/1960" title="1960">1960</a> – <a href="/wiki/2_May" title="2 May">2 May</a>, <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>), also known as <b>Moony</b>, was a <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> and the only son of <a href="/wiki/Lyall_Lupin" title="Lyall Lupin">Lyall</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hope_Howell" title="Hope Howell">Hope Lupin</a> <span class="template-c">(née Howell)</span>. He was attacked by <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> when he was a child, a result of Greyback's revenge against Lyall, leaving Remus afflicted with <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">Lycanthropy</a> for life. He attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> from <a href="/wiki/1971" title="1971">1971</a>-<a href="/wiki/1978" title="1978">1978</a> and was <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorted</a> into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>. During his school years he was one of the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>, best friends with <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>. Together, they created the <a href="/wiki/Marauder%27s_Map" title="Marauder&#39;s Map">Marauder's Map</a>.
</p><p>After Hogwarts, Remus and his friends joined the original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and fought in the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. However, Pettigrew betrayed James and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a> to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> a week after he was made the couples' <a href="/wiki/Secret_Keeper" title="Secret Keeper">Secret Keeper</a>. Thus Remus had lost all of his closest friends in various ways by the end of the First Wizarding War. The loss of his friends devastated him, though he and Sirius Black later rekindled their friendship. 
</p><p>Remus taught at Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry as Professor of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> during the <a href="/wiki/1993-1994_school_year" class="mw-redirect" title="1993-1994 school year">1993-1994 school year</a>. Remus was regarded by students to be the best Defence teacher they have had thus far. He was also a professor of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> (James' son) whom he taught how to conjure a corporeal <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a>, but resigned after <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> revealed to the public that Remus was a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a>. 
</p><p>He fought against <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> once more in the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, during which he lost his friend Sirius. In <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Remus married fellow Order member <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a> and had a son, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Edward Remus Lupin</a>, of whom he named Harry the godfather. Remus fought at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> on <a href="/wiki/2_May" title="2 May">2 May</a>, <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, during which his wife was murdered by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. Remus was also murdered by Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>, during the first half of the same battle. His death was avenged by <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>.
</p><p>Remus briefly appeared again through the <a href="/wiki/Resurrection_Stone" title="Resurrection Stone">Resurrection Stone</a> for Harry, along with James Potter, Lily Potter, and Sirius Black in 1998. After his death, his son was raised by <a href="/wiki/Andromeda_Tonks" title="Andromeda Tonks">Andromeda Tonks</a> and Harry Potter.
</p>
