<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Early_life_(1960-1971)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_.281960-1971.29">Early life <span class="template-c">(1960-1971)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life (1960-1971)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early life (1960-1971)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Remus was born on <a href="/wiki/10_March" title="10 March">10 March</a>, <a href="/wiki/1960" title="1960">1960</a> to <a href="/wiki/Lyall_Lupin" title="Lyall Lupin">Lyall</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hope_Howell" title="Hope Howell">Hope Lupin</a>. His father worked at the Ministry of Magic and encountered the werewolf <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>, who was on trial for killing two children. Lyall was the only one at court to realise that Greyback was a werewolf, as Greyback pretended to be a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> tramp. Outraged when Greyback was released, he voiced the opinion that Greyback deserved nothing but death. This opinion cost the Lupin family dearly, as Greyback decided to revenge himself upon Lyall by targeting his son. As the nearly five-year-old Remus slept peacefully in his bed, Greyback forced his way in through the window. Though Lyall was able to get there in time to drive Greyback off with powerful spells, he was unable to prevent him from completing his evil goal. Remus became infected with <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">lycanthropy</a> and he became a werewolf himself.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>His parents took him to various healers and tried their best to make him a normal boy, but there was no cure for his condition. But Headmaster <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> made special accommodations allowing Remus to attend <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Hogwarts_years_(1971-1978)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years_.281971-1978.29">Hogwarts years <span class="template-c">(1971-1978)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1971-1978)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1971-1978)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>My transformations in those days were — were terrible. It is very painful to turn into a werewolf. I was separated from humans to bite, so I bit and scratched myself instead. The villagers heard the noise and the screaming and thought they were hearing particularly violent spirits.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Description of Lupin's transformations<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Sorting_Ceremony_1971.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151231020312" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="109" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sorting Ceremony 1971.jpg" data-image-key="Sorting_Ceremony_1971.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Sorting_Ceremony_1971.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151231020312" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Sorting_Ceremony_1971.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151231020312" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Sorting_Ceremony_1971.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151231020312" decoding="async" width="250" height="109" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sorting Ceremony 1971.jpg" data-image-key="Sorting_Ceremony_1971.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Sorting_Ceremony_1971.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151231020312" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sorting_Ceremony_1971.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus' Sorting in 1971, where he was Sorted into Gryffindor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus attended Hogwarts and was Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>. To secure his safety, as well as that of his peers, Remus would be brought to the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a> once a month for his transformations in order to prevent him from attacking other students. However, this isolation caused him to attack himself out of frustration. This, and the painful monthly transformations, made the villagers of <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> mistake his screams for that of violent <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">ghosts</a>. Dumbledore, wanting to keep the truth of these noises a secret, encouraged these rumours. Thus, the building was dubbed the Shrieking Shack, which held the reputation for being the most haunted building in Britain.<sup id="cite_ref-POA18_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA18-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Remus became the very best of friends with fellow Gryffindors <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>. He kept his status as a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> a secret from all of the students at Hogwarts, including Sirius, James, and Peter, his fellow Marauders and future Order members. He made up stories to explain his monthly disappearances, such as that his mother was ill and he needed to go home to visit her. He was terrified that they would desert him once they found out what he truly was. However, Sirius, James, and Peter worked out the truth during their second year, and due to their acceptance of who Remus was, and their unusually strong friendship with him, they decided to learn how to become <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagi</a> in order to keep Remus company during his transformations, as a werewolf is only a danger to humans.<sup id="cite_ref-POA18_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA18-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/64/Marauders.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170911010102" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marauders.jpg" data-image-key="Marauders.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/64/Marauders.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170911010102" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/64/Marauders.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170911010102" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/64/Marauders.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170911010102" decoding="async" width="250" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marauders.jpg" data-image-key="Marauders.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/64/Marauders.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170911010102" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marauders.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Marauders in their Animagus forms, Lupin as a werewolf, on the far left</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>By their fifth year, Sirius was able to become a <a href="/wiki/Dog" title="Dog">dog</a>, and James was able to become a <a href="/wiki/Deer" title="Deer">stag</a>, animals large enough to keep the wolfish Remus in check. Peter, meanwhile, was able to become a <a href="/wiki/Rat" title="Rat">rat</a>. Once a month during the full moon, Sirius, James and Peter would sneak out of the castle under James' <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility Cloak</a>, transform, get into the <a href="/wiki/Whomping_Willow" title="Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a>, walk down the tunnel and meet up with Remus in the Shrieking Shack. Under their influence, Lupin became tame; his body was still a wolf's, but his mind became less so when he was among them. The four of them soon left the Whomping Willow and would roam among the school grounds and <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> by night. Eventually, this group of friends came to call themselves the Marauders, and Remus' friends nicknamed him "Moony" because of his transformations during every full <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">moon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Remus was a good student, but also a prankster. He and Peter Pettigrew would sometimes join Sirius and James in detention for mischief-making, though they did not get into as much trouble as their other friends. It's unlikely that any other Hogwarts students ever found out as much about the Hogwarts grounds and <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> as they did and Sirius, James, Remus and Peter used their knowledge of it to write the <a href="/wiki/Marauder%27s_Map" title="Marauder&#39;s Map">Marauder's Map</a> and signed it with their nicknames.<sup id="cite_ref-POA18_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA18-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Unfortunately, it somehow ended up being confiscated by <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, but was eventually recovered by <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a> in the 1989-90 school year.<sup id="cite_ref-POA10_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA10-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bd/Mauraders.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161127052833" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mauraders.jpg" data-image-key="Mauraders.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bd/Mauraders.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161127052833" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bd/Mauraders.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161127052833" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bd/Mauraders.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161127052833" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mauraders.jpg" data-image-key="Mauraders.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bd/Mauraders.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161127052833" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mauraders.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a> in their final years at Hogwarts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, Remus' frequent disappearances riled up an unhealthy curiosity in <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> student whom the Marauders often bullied, in the same year as Remus. Because of Severus' enmity towards Sirius and James, he disliked Remus and Peter by association, making him all the more suspicious. He often followed Sirius, James, Remus, and Peter around in order to see what they were up to and in an effort to have them expelled.<sup id="cite_ref-POA18_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA18-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime in their fifth-year<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>, Sirius played a malicious prank on Snape by telling him about the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Whomping_Willow" title="Hogwarts Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a> passageway, hoping that he would be terrified or even get seriously hurt by what he found at the other end. James, who hated Snape, was able to stop Snape and save his life in the nick of time, but Snape still uncovered Remus' secret, seeing him at the end of the passage.
</p><p>Remus was also a <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefect</a> while he was at Hogwarts, although he had trouble exercising discipline over his dearest friend due to loyalty. He claimed Albus Dumbledore had hoped he could exert control over them as a Prefect. Sirius later told Harry that Remus wasn't an idiot like his friends because he was never cruel to Snape. But Remus admitted that he regretted that he had never stepped in to stop it.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h3><span id="First_Wizarding_War_(1978-1981)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="First_Wizarding_War_.281978-1981.29">First Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1978-1981)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First Wizarding War (1978-1981)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: First Wizarding War (1978-1981)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Remus</b>: "<i>...he thought I was the spy, Peter. I assume that's why you didn't tell me, Sirius?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Sirius Black</b>: "<i>Forgive me, Remus.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Remus</b>: "<i>Not at all, Padfoot, old friend. And will you forgive me for believing you were the spy?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Sirius Black</b>: "<i>Of course.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Reflecting on the First Wizarding War<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720155740" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Marauders in Order of the Pheonix image.jpg" data-image-key="The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720155740" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720155740" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720155740" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Marauders in Order of the Pheonix image.jpg" data-image-key="The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720155740" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus (far left) during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shortly after graduating from Hogwarts, Remus joined the Order of the Phoenix along with Sirius, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>, standing up against <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. Remus failed to find employment following his education because of his affliction as a werewolf. However, James used his wealth to financially support him.<sup id="cite_ref-CarnegieHall_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CarnegieHall-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>By the height of the war, Remus' friend <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> had come to distrust him, suspecting that he might be a spy for the other side. Thus, when a <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">prophecy</a> was made about a child who would have the power to defeat the Dark Lord, and Dumbledore identified infant <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> as a possible target, Remus was not included in the plan to keep the <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potters</a> safe, though he was aware that they used the <a href="/wiki/Fidelius_Charm" title="Fidelius Charm">Fidelius Charm</a>. James and Lily Potter wanted to use Sirius as their <a href="/wiki/Secret-Keeper" class="mw-redirect" title="Secret-Keeper">Secret-Keeper</a>, but Sirius thought that would be too obvious, and thus suggested Peter Pettigrew instead, who would be a nearly unpredictable move, him being known for his "<i>measly empty-headedness</i>." Neither Dumbledore or Lupin knew of this switch.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the time of Lily and James' death, Lupin was in the north of the country on <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> business when he discovered what had, apparently, happened. This was one of the most traumatic events of Remus' life, especially since, within the next day, he would also be losing his other two best friends. Sirius was imprisoned in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for supposedly murdering Pettigrew and twelve Muggles with one <a href="/wiki/Blasting_Curse" title="Blasting Curse">curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Between_the_wars_(1981-1994)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Between_the_wars_.281981-1994.29">Between the wars <span class="template-c">(1981-1994)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Between the wars (1981-1994)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Between the wars (1981-1994)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Deal_with_Chiara_Lobosca">Deal with Chiara Lobosca</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Deal with Chiara Lobosca">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Deal with Chiara Lobosca"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After Voldemort's first downfall, the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> disbanded, and members returned to their busy lives with their families. Lupin, however, was left lonely and unhappy — two of his three best friends were dead, one was imprisoned for mass murder, his mother had eventually died too, and he refused to spoil his father's peaceful existence by returning to live with him. Remus was forced to take jobs that were far below his level of ability, always knowing he would have to leave them before his workmates noticed the signs of his lycanthropy. A faint ray of hope came for Remus when he heard of the new invention of the <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a>, which can mitigate the worst effects of lycanthropy, though this was almost immediately dashed when he saw the potion's complexity and expensive ingredients. Potions was not his strongest suit and he has a very low income rate.
</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Remus_Lupin_and_Chiara_Lobosca.png/revision/latest?cb=20191102172006" class="image"><img alt="Remus Lupin and Chiara Lobosca.png" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus Lupin and Chiara Lobosca.png" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_and_Chiara_Lobosca.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Remus_Lupin_and_Chiara_Lobosca.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20191102172006" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Remus_Lupin_and_Chiara_Lobosca.png/revision/latest?cb=20191102172006" class="image"><img alt="Remus Lupin and Chiara Lobosca.png" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Remus_Lupin_and_Chiara_Lobosca.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20191102172006" decoding="async" width="180" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus Lupin and Chiara Lobosca.png" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_and_Chiara_Lobosca.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Remus_Lupin_and_Chiara_Lobosca.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20191102172006" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_Lupin_and_Chiara_Lobosca.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>
While unable to afford the potion nor its ingredients, Lupin thought to search for the latter in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>, where he ran into Hogwarts student <a href="/wiki/Chiara_Lobosca" title="Chiara Lobosca">Chiara Lobosca</a>, whom he was able to get the potion from on a few occasions. They would meet each night for a week before a full moon, during which Chiara would give Lupin a bottle of potion.<sup id="cite_ref-chiara3_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-chiara3-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/1985%E2%80%931986_school_year" title="1985–1986 school year">1985–1986 school year</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ben_Copper" title="Ben Copper">Ben Copper</a> witnessed a potion transaction between the two upon inquiry, Lobosca admitted that, unbeknownst to Lupin, she was giving Lupin potions made for her since the ingredients were only enough to make the dosage for one person and she felt he needed them more than she did.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Upon hearing this, Lupin, who had been led to believe that her supply of Wolfsbane Potion was such that she just had plenty to share, reluctantly accepted this last potion from her, but then refused in advance to accept any more.<sup id="cite_ref-chiara3_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-chiara3-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Becoming_a_professor">Becoming a professor</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Becoming a professor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Becoming a professor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Nothing to worry about. There’s a Boggart in there. Boggarts like dark, enclosed spaces. Wardrobes, the gap beneath beds, the cupboards under sinks — I’ve even met one that had lodged itself in a grandfather clock. This one moved in yesterday afternoon, and I asked the headmaster if the staff would leave it to give my third years some practise.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Remus Lupin teaching third year DADA students about <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggarts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 156px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Normal_poa_%2823%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140518055531" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="154" height="237" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Normal poa (23).jpg" data-image-key="Normal_poa_(23).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Normal_poa_%2823%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20140518055531" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Normal_poa_%2823%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140518055531" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Normal_poa_%2823%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20140518055531" decoding="async" width="154" height="237" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Normal poa (23).jpg" data-image-key="Normal_poa_(23).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Normal_poa_%2823%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20140518055531" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Normal_poa_(23).jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus as Defence Against the Dark Arts professor, <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>By the early <a href="/wiki/1990s" title="1990s">1990s</a>, Lupin was living in poverty, in a tumbledown, semi-derelict cottage in Yorkshire. <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> tracked Lupin down in the summer of 1993, and offered him the post of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> Professor at Hogwarts, replacing the permanently amnesiac <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>. Lupin only accepted Dumbledore's proposal when he explained there would be a limitless supply of <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a>, courtesy of Severus Snape, now the <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> at the school.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/LupinExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190416104624" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="LupinExpectoPatronum.gif" data-image-key="LupinExpectoPatronum.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/LupinExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190416104624" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/LupinExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190416104624" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/LupinExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190416104624" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="LupinExpectoPatronum.gif" data-image-key="LupinExpectoPatronum.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/LupinExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190416104624" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:LupinExpectoPatronum.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus fending off Dementor that boarded the Hogwarts Express in search of Sirius Black</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> 
<p>Lupin travelled to Hogwarts via the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>. It was here where Remus first directly met <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. Lupin was apparently sleeping so deeply that he did not notice Hermione's attempt to wake him up to buy some food from the <a href="/wiki/Honeydukes_Express" title="Honeydukes Express">Honeydukes Express</a>, but swiftly awoke to deal with a <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementor</a> who was prowling in their cabin in search for the runaway Sirius. Remus disguised his <a href="/wiki/Wolf" title="Wolf">wolf</a>-shaped <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> as a vague mist to prevent leaving hints about his afflictions. He then gave everybody within the compartment a piece of <a href="/wiki/Chocolate" title="Chocolate">chocolate</a>, as a mild relief from the Dementor's effects. While doing so he greeted Harry in a casual and friendly fashion.<sup id="cite_ref-POA5_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA5-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Although Remus did not receive much enthusiasm from most students' applause during his introduction due to his rather shabby appearance, Harry and his friends were the few who gave their full approval due to the positive first impression he gave them. The students were kept in the dark about his affliction, but the staff were made aware that he was a werewolf. <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, who had switched sides at the end of the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">war</a> and became <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> Professor, provided Remus with Wolfsbane Potion, allowing him to retain his human mind during transformations.<sup id="cite_ref-POA18_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA18-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Remus taught the class a comprehensive and fascinating curriculum of identifying and sidestepping Dark creatures such as <a href="/wiki/Hinkypunk" title="Hinkypunk">Hinkypunks</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA10_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA10-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Red_Cap" title="Red Cap">Red Caps</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA8_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA8-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Kappa" title="Kappa">Kappas</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA8_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA8-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Grindylow" title="Grindylow">Grindylows</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA8_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA8-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Vampire" title="Vampire">Vampires</a>, <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">Werewolves</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nocturnal_beasts" title="Nocturnal beasts">Nocturnal beasts</a>. He also taught the class about <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggarts</a>, and how to repel them using the <a href="/wiki/Boggart-Banishing_Spell" title="Boggart-Banishing Spell">Boggart-Banishing Spell</a>, to great success.<sup id="cite_ref-POA7_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA7-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Remus had proven himself a skilled teacher, managing to keep the children's' interest in the subject and had shown himself far more competent than his predecessor's vain, useless lessons. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/B3C12M1_Remus_Harry_Anti-Dementor_lessons.png/revision/latest?cb=20161208054533" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B3C12M1 Remus Harry Anti-Dementor lessons.png" data-image-key="B3C12M1_Remus_Harry_Anti-Dementor_lessons.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/B3C12M1_Remus_Harry_Anti-Dementor_lessons.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161208054533" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/B3C12M1_Remus_Harry_Anti-Dementor_lessons.png/revision/latest?cb=20161208054533" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/B3C12M1_Remus_Harry_Anti-Dementor_lessons.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161208054533" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B3C12M1 Remus Harry Anti-Dementor lessons.png" data-image-key="B3C12M1_Remus_Harry_Anti-Dementor_lessons.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/B3C12M1_Remus_Harry_Anti-Dementor_lessons.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161208054533" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B3C12M1_Remus_Harry_Anti-Dementor_lessons.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry Potter's first lesson on the <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> 
<p>It was during their Boggart class that <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> realised his "<i>greatest fear was fear itself</i>" when his <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a> took on the form of a <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementor</a>. After this, Remus gave Harry private lessons in producing a <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> as a means to repel <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>, when it became apparent that he was especially vulnerable to them because, according to Lupin, Harry had "true horrors" in his past that were especially appealing to the Dementors.<sup id="cite_ref-POA12_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA12-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Incidentally, being a werewolf, Remus' Boggart would take on the form of the full moon. Students who saw this Boggart form mistook it for a crystal ball, except for <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, who cleverly deduced that Remus was a werewolf and kept the discovery to herself.<sup id="cite_ref-POA17_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA17-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> students, encouraged by <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, sneered at Remus' shabby clothes and poor appearance, although he seemed to ignore their comments.<sup id="cite_ref-POA8_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA8-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Regardless, his other students held him in extremely high regard and loved the hands-on style of his classes. He was considered by Harry and his friends to have been their only decent Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/PM-templ.png/revision/latest?cb=20140713000638" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="PM-templ.png" data-image-key="PM-templ.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/PM-templ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140713000638" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/PM-templ.png/revision/latest?cb=20140713000638" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/PM-templ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140713000638" decoding="async" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="PM-templ.png" data-image-key="PM-templ.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/PM-templ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140713000638" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:PM-templ.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lupin in Professor Snape's fireplace, having used <a href="/wiki/Floo_Powder" title="Floo Powder">Floo Powder</a> to get there</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus was soon summoned to Snape's office to identify whether a piece of parchment he caught Harry with to be Dark magic. Remus recognised it as the Marauder's Map but tried to pass it off as a product of <a href="/wiki/Zonko%27s_Joke_Shop" title="Zonko&#39;s Joke Shop">Zonko's Joke Shop</a>. At the same moment, Ron burst in to back up that claim. After escorting the two boys from Snape's office, Remus told them that he knew what the map was and was more astounded that they did not hand it in, and reprimanded Harry, much to their surprise. He confiscated the map, knowing that it would be too dangerous for Harry to use the secret passages with Sirius on the loose.<sup id="cite_ref-POA14_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA14-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>For his third years' end of year tests in June, he prepared an unusual exam — an obstacle course out in the grounds in which the students had to: wade across a paddling pool containing a <a href="/wiki/Grindylow" title="Grindylow">grindylow</a>; cross a series of pot-holes full of Red Caps; cross a marsh while being fed misleading directions by a hinkypunk; and enter a trunk to battle a newly procured boggart.<sup id="cite_ref-POA16_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA16-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Hermione Granger even commented in her fifth year that Lupin's exam was the only occasion where she and Harry took a Defence exam from a teacher who knew what they were doing (exams were cancelled in second year and Harry was exempt due to his status as a Triwizard Champion in fourth year). 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Exposure_of_Peter_Pettigrew">Exposure of Peter Pettigrew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Exposure of Peter Pettigrew">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Exposure of Peter Pettigrew"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Lupin</b>: "<i>Didn’t you ever hear, Ron? The biggest bit of Peter they found was his finger.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i> Look, Scabbers probably had a fight with another rat or something! He’s been in my family for ages, right —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Lupin</b>: "<i>Twelve years, in fact. Didn’t you ever wonder why he was living so long?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Lupin exposing Peter Pettigrew as an Animagus<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>The summer before Remus began his tenure as the Defence professor, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> escaped from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>. Remus, like the rest of the wizarding world, believed that Sirius had betrayed the <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potters</a> to Voldemort and murdered Peter Pettigrew.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/ff/52775.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140520190737" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="52775.jpg" data-image-key="52775.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/ff/52775.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20140520190737" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/ff/52775.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140520190737" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/ff/52775.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20140520190737" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="52775.jpg" data-image-key="52775.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/ff/52775.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20140520190737" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:52775.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus Lupin, Sirius Black and Scabbers (Pettigrew) in the Shrieking Shack</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>By the end of the school year, however, Remus knew the truth of what had happened and that Pettigrew was still alive, hiding in his <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> form — <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Scabbers</a>, the pet rat of <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>. He was watching the Marauder's Map, expecting Harry and his friends to go down to see Hagrid before <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>'s execution and was shocked to see Pettigrew coming out of Hagrid's with them. Remus was reunited with his old friend Sirius, and the two resolved to kill Pettigrew for his part in the deaths of James and Lily and in framing Sirius. They were stopped by Harry Potter, who believed it would be better to hand Pettigrew over to the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> to prove Sirius' innocence, and also did not think his father would want Remus and Sirius to become killers.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>There was a terrible snarling noise. Lupin’s head was lengthening. So was his body. His shoulders were hunching. Hair was sprouting visibly on his face and hands, which were curling into clawed paws.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin transforming into a werewolf under the moonlight<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Remus_Lupin_turning_into_Werewolf.gif/revision/latest?cb=20090305025725" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="108" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus Lupin turning into Werewolf.gif" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_turning_into_Werewolf.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Remus_Lupin_turning_into_Werewolf.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20090305025725" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Remus_Lupin_turning_into_Werewolf.gif/revision/latest?cb=20090305025725" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Remus_Lupin_turning_into_Werewolf.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20090305025725" decoding="async" width="220" height="108" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus Lupin turning into Werewolf.gif" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_turning_into_Werewolf.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Remus_Lupin_turning_into_Werewolf.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20090305025725" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_Lupin_turning_into_Werewolf.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus transforms into a werewolf</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, that night happened to be a full moon, and Remus transformed into a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> (having forgotten to take the <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a>). Sirius was forced to turn into his Animagus form to protect Harry, Ron and Hermione from Remus. In the chaos, Pettigrew unfortunately escaped and would later return to his master. After the attempted attack on Harry and Hermione, Remus spent the rest of the night deep in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Resignation">Resignation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Resignation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Resignation"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>This time tomorrow, the <a href="/wiki/Owl" title="Owl">owls</a> will start arriving from parents... They will not want a werewolf teaching their children, Harry. And after last night, I see their point. I could have bitten any of you... That must never happen again.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin explaining his resignation to Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png/revision/latest?cb=20180420201420" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B3C22M1 Lupin leaving his office and teaching post.png" data-image-key="B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420201420" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png/revision/latest?cb=20180420201420" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420201420" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B3C22M1 Lupin leaving his office and teaching post.png" data-image-key="B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420201420" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry Potter and Dumbledore seeing Remus off</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the danger had passed, Remus resigned from his position when parents learned that he was a werewolf. His sudden resignation was much to the regret of the majority of the Hogwarts students and staff, who had all grown deeply fond of him.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Harry, in particular, begged him earnestly to stay, declaring that he was the best Defence Against The Dark Arts teacher that the students had ever had. Remus simply shook his head, handed him the Marauder's Map and also returned the <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility Cloak</a> that was left at the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>, and told him that it had been a real pleasure teaching him, and that he was perfectly sure that they would soon meet again.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He sent a letter to his successor informing him of what he taught Harry and the others, but it was <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">intercepted</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF14_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF14-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Second_Wizarding_War_(1995-1998)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_Wizarding_War_.281995-1998.29">Second Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1995-1998)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995-1998)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995-1998)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>They’re trying to discredit him. Didn’t you see the Daily Prophet last week? They reported that he’d been voted out of the Chairmanship of the International Confederation of Wizards because he’s getting old and losing his grip, but it’s not true, he was voted out by Ministry wizards after he made a speech announcing Voldemort’s return. They’ve demoted him from Chief Warlock on the Wizengamot — that’s the Wizard High Court — and they’re talking about taking away his Order of Merlin, First Class, too.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Remus regarding the Minister's denial of Voldemort's return<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order_of_the_Pheonix.png/revision/latest?cb=20190209172140" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Pheonix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Pheonix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order_of_the_Pheonix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190209172140" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order_of_the_Pheonix.png/revision/latest?cb=20190209172140" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order_of_the_Pheonix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190209172140" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Pheonix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Pheonix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order_of_the_Pheonix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190209172140" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Pheonix.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">An Order meeting taking place at 12 Grimmauld Place</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> returned, Remus rejoined the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. He was a member of the <a href="/wiki/Advance_Guard" title="Advance Guard">Advance Guard</a> that escorted Harry Potter from <a href="/wiki/4_Privet_Drive" title="4 Privet Drive">4 Privet Drive</a> to <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a>. Lupin lived for some time at Sirius' house, but he was not around very often as he was usually sent on many missions for the Order.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Lupin_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190820192021" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="90" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lupin Grimmauld Place.jpg" data-image-key="Lupin_Grimmauld_Place.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Lupin_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190820192021" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Lupin_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190820192021" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Lupin_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190820192021" decoding="async" width="220" height="90" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lupin Grimmauld Place.jpg" data-image-key="Lupin_Grimmauld_Place.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Lupin_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190820192021" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lupin_Grimmauld_Place.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lupin arguing with Harry at 12 Grimmauld Place</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During Christmas, <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> had been attacked by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s snake, <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP22_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP22-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Remus once visited him at <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a> along with Harry, Hermione, and the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasleys</a><a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">.</a> Remus strolled over to the <a href="/wiki/Unidentified_werewolf" title="Unidentified werewolf">Unidentified werewolf</a> and spoke to him for a while, most likely to tell him about <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">lycanthropy</a> and console him over his new condition. He gave Harry along with Sirius a set of excellent books enti­tled <a href="/wiki/Practical_Defensive_Magic_and_Its_Use_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Practical Defensive Magic and Its Use Against the Dark Arts">Practical Defensive Magic and Its Use Against the Dark Arts</a> as a Christmas present.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP23_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP23-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Lupin, along with <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Tonks</a>, escorted Harry, Hermione, and the Weasley children back to Hogwarts on the <a href="/wiki/Knight_Bus" title="Knight Bus">Knight Bus</a> to start the new term.
</p><p>Remus also accompanied Sirius in conversation with Harry through the fireplace at Grimmauld Place, when Harry used the <a href="/wiki/Floo_Powder" title="Floo Powder">Floo Powder</a> from the fireplace in <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts_teacher%27s_office" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher&#39;s office">Dolores Umbridge's office</a> to talk with Black about his father James and Snape's memory, which he saw in the <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a>. Lupin, like Sirius, did not hide his indignation when he learned that Snape had stopped teaching Harry the <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP29_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP29-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Department of Mysteries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Battle of the Department of Mysteries"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Harry, round up the others and GO!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin to Harry Potter during the Battle of the Department of Mysteries<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140616001834" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Battle of the Department of Mysteries GIF.gif" data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140616001834" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140616001834" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140616001834" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Battle of the Department of Mysteries GIF.gif" data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140616001834" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries_GIF.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus duelling a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> in the Death Chamber of the Department of Mysteries</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/18_June" title="18 June">18 June</a> 1996, Remus participated in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> and defeated a number of Death Eaters including their leader, <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>. He was one of the only three combatants to see the end of the battle unscathed, the others being <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, proving Remus' exceptional skill at duelling. During this battle, Remus witnessed and was devastated by the death of his last surviving Marauder friend, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a>, who was pushed through the <a href="/wiki/Veil" title="Veil">veil</a> in the Death Chamber by a <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange%27s_unidentified_spell" title="Bellatrix Lestrange&#39;s unidentified spell">spell</a> cast by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP35_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP35-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Remus barely managed to prevent Harry from diving in after Sirius, who was already lost.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP36_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP36-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Shortly after the battle and the end of school year, Remus along with Moody, Tonks and Weasleys confronted the Dursleys at <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Cross" class="mw-redirect" title="King&#39;s Cross">King's Cross</a> station over their treatment of Harry.<sup id="cite_ref-ootp38_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ootp38-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Underground">Underground</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Underground">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Underground"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Some weeks later, Remus began working as a spy for the Order, living among fellow <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolves</a> and trying to convince them to join Dumbledore's side. It is said that he volunteered just to keep away from Tonks, as they were both very much in love with each other by this point and he would not risk his child having lycanthropy. Alas, it was difficult to convince them due to the fact that they believed they will have a better life under Voldemort's reign, many were frightened and intimidated by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> and that Remus showed signs of living among humans.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Weeks later, on Harry's 16th birthday, Remus visited <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">The Burrow</a> with news of Dementor attacks and murder of <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-hbp6_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hbp6-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0e/Lupin_Burrow2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190820192442" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lupin Burrow2.jpg" data-image-key="Lupin_Burrow2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0e/Lupin_Burrow2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190820192442" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0e/Lupin_Burrow2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190820192442" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0e/Lupin_Burrow2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190820192442" decoding="async" width="220" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lupin Burrow2.jpg" data-image-key="Lupin_Burrow2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0e/Lupin_Burrow2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190820192442" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lupin_Burrow2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lupin arguing with Harry, Tonks and Arthur during Christmas at the Burrow</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> 
<p>During Christmas at the Burrow, Harry told Remus and Arthur Weasley about the  conversation he overheard between <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. Mr Weasley immediately suggested that Snape was just pretending to help Malfoy, but Lupin severely pointed out that Dumbledore trusted Snape, which "ought to be good enough for all of them." Although Snape exposed Lupin as a werewolf, forcing him to resign his position at Hogwarts, he also kept him healthy by making him a special potion during his monthly transformation. Lupin neither liked nor disliked Snape – but personal feelings have nothing to do with his decision to trust him. Lupin argued strongly against making judgments based on feelings – even though he, of all people, had strong reasons to dislike Snape personally, he refused to let this affect his conclusions about the man. This pronouncement established him as a foil to <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a> and Sirius, who disliked Snape for petty reasons and treated these feelings as a justification for bullying him. 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>NO!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin's loss of control upon hearing of Dumbledore's death<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c9/Dumbledore_funeral.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091001180833" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore funeral.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_funeral.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c9/Dumbledore_funeral.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20091001180833" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c9/Dumbledore_funeral.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091001180833" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c9/Dumbledore_funeral.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20091001180833" decoding="async" width="220" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore funeral.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_funeral.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c9/Dumbledore_funeral.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20091001180833" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_funeral.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The funeral of Albus Dumbledore</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The following year, Remus fought bravely again at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> where he narrowly avoided death by a <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">curse</a> from <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a>. Remus, was devastated upon hearing about the death of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, who had been killed by Severus Snape. However, the aftermath of the battle led to him to accept the love of <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, who pointed out that <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> still loved <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a> in spite of being attacked and scarred by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>. The pair attended their former Headmaster's <a href="/wiki/Funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Funeral of Albus Dumbledore">funeral</a> together.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marriage">Marriage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Marriage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Marriage"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Shortly after Dumbledore's funeral and some days before the Order operation to transport Harry from his relative's home to safety, Remus and Tonks soon married in the north of Scotland with only witnesses from the local tavern.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Lupin, same as Tonks, was sad that Harry didn't attend their wedding, because he couldn't leave the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursleys</a> home, due Lily's <a href="/wiki/Sacrificial_protection" title="Sacrificial protection">loving sacrifice</a> when she willingly died for her only son. They were forced to marry quietly, given the general prejudice against werewolves.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Remus, to his surprise, learned that his wife got pregnant some time after the wedding.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Seven Potters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Battle of the Seven Potters"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Harry, the time for <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming</a> is past! These people are trying to capture and kill you! At least stun if you aren't prepared to kill!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Remus scolds Harry Potter for showing mercy during the sky battle<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/DH1_Fleur%2C_Bill_Weasley%2C_Nymphadora%2C_Remus_Lupin_and_Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817175816" class="image"><img alt="" decoding="async" width="220" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 Fleur, Bill Weasley, Nymphadora, Remus Lupin and Harry Potter.jpg" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_Fleur,_Bill_Weasley,_Nymphadora,_Remus_Lupin_and_Harry_Potter.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus, Tonks and Order of Phoenix members at 4 Privet Drive</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/27_July" title="27 July">27th July</a> 1997, Remus participated in the Order's operation to remove Harry from his home before <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> could get to him. Remus acted as the protector of <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>, who took <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> to become one of the "seven Potters." The party was ambushed by at least thirty cloaked <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH4_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH4-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> George was accidentally struck by Severus Snape, who was trying to aim for a Death Eater, but accidentally stuck George instead with his <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> curse while George and Remus flew. Lupin was unable to pay Snape back in time, it being all he could do to keep George on the broom, as the latter was losing a copious amount of blood.<sup id="cite_ref-DH5_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH5-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
