<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/7alupin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817171127" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="7alupin.jpg" data-image-key="7alupin.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/7alupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190817171127" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/7alupin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817171127" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/7alupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190817171127" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="7alupin.jpg" data-image-key="7alupin.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/7alupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190817171127" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:7alupin.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus making sure that Harry is not an impostor in the Burrow's kitchen after the sky battle</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He eventually got the injured George back to <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">The Burrow</a> to be cleaned up, though George permanently lost an ear. Upon arrival, Remus accosted Harry to prove that Harry was the real Harry. It was later revealed that Snape had sent the spell in an attempt to cut off the hand of a Death Eater aiming at Remus' back, presumably about to kill him. Remus was very anxious about the late arrival of his wife; Tonks had been aggressively pursued by her murderous, cruel aunt, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. When the party mourned the death of fellow order member <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, they discussed their betrayal. Harry voiced the opinion that he trusted all of them with his life. Remus urged caution, seeing as Harry's father was killed because he put his trust in the wrong friend.<sup id="cite_ref-DH5_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH5-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wedding_of_Bill_and_Fleur">Wedding of Bill and Fleur</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Wedding of Bill and Fleur">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Wedding of Bill and Fleur"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Attack_at_Burrow-Remus.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140523152501" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Attack at Burrow-Remus.jpg" data-image-key="Attack_at_Burrow-Remus.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Attack_at_Burrow-Remus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20140523152501" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Attack_at_Burrow-Remus.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140523152501" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Attack_at_Burrow-Remus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20140523152501" decoding="async" width="220" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Attack at Burrow-Remus.jpg" data-image-key="Attack_at_Burrow-Remus.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Attack_at_Burrow-Remus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20140523152501" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Attack_at_Burrow-Remus.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus defending the Burrow</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the next days Remus seemed to become withdrawn and sullen at the news. He awhile attended <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_seventeenth_birthday" title="Harry Potter&#39;s seventeenth birthday">Harry's birthday party</a>, but left when <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a> has arrived. Remus and Tonks both later attended the <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">wedding</a> of <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> shortly afterwards, and bravely defended the Burrow when it came under attack as Voldemort took over the Ministry.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Remus along with Tonks both used a <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a>. It is unknown as to whether he escaped, or he was questioned by the intruders, along with the other guests, before being released.<sup id="cite_ref-DH9_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH9-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="On_the_run">On the run</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: On the run">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: On the run"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Don't you understand what I've done to my wife and <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">my unborn child</a>? I should never have married her, I've made her an outcast! And the child — the child...my kind don't usually breed! It will be like me, I am convinced of it! How can I forgive myself when I knowingly risked passing on my own condition to an innocent child?! And if, by some miracle, it is not like me, then it will be better off, a hundred </i>times<i> so, without a father of whom it should always be ashamed!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Remus' view of his marriage to Tonks and her pregnancy<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 187px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Remuslupin_DH.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090316073657" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="185" height="216" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remuslupin DH.jpg" data-image-key="Remuslupin_DH.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Remuslupin_DH.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/185?cb=20090316073657" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Remuslupin_DH.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090316073657" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Remuslupin_DH.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/185?cb=20090316073657" decoding="async" width="185" height="216" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remuslupin DH.jpg" data-image-key="Remuslupin_DH.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Remuslupin_DH.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/185?cb=20090316073657" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remuslupin_DH.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus visiting the trio in 12 Grimmauld Place, while on the run</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus suffered great mental anguish as the war escalated when he learned that his wife was pregnant. He even tore out a clump of his own hair in anxiety over the possibility that his child would be born a werewolf. He visited Harry, Ron, and Hermione while they hid out in <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">Grimmauld Place</a> and offered to help with their search for Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>. However, Harry denounced him, calling him a coward for even considering leaving his wife alone while pregnant. Remus got so mad that he flung Harry against the wall with his wand, and left, greatly agitated.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Harry and his friends next heard of Remus on <i><a href="/wiki/Potterwatch" title="Potterwatch">Potterwatch</a></i>, under the code name "Romulus". Remus made Harry realise that they were still good friends, with his putting forth the opinion that Harry's instincts were good and they were usually right.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Remus eventually came to his senses and reunited with Tonks in time to see his son's birth. They named him Edward Remus "Teddy" Lupin, after Tonks' father, who had recently been murdered by <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a> after refusing to turn himself in to the <a href="/wiki/Muggle-Born_Registration_Commission" title="Muggle-Born Registration Commission">Muggle-Born Registration Commission</a>. Appearing to forgive and forget their earlier disagreement in Grimmauld Place, Remus asked Harry to be Teddy's godfather.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts_and_death"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> and death</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts and death">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts and death"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Nymphadora Tonks</b>: "<i>Have you seen Remus? </i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Aberforth Dumbledore</b>: "<i>He was duelling Dolohov, haven't seen him since!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Right before Lupin's murder at the hands of Dolohov<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Tonks_and_Lupin_preparing_for_battle.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110511111040" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="108" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tonks and Lupin preparing for battle.gif" data-image-key="Tonks_and_Lupin_preparing_for_battle.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Tonks_and_Lupin_preparing_for_battle.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20110511111040" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Tonks_and_Lupin_preparing_for_battle.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110511111040" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Tonks_and_Lupin_preparing_for_battle.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20110511111040" decoding="async" width="245" height="108" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tonks and Lupin preparing for battle.gif" data-image-key="Tonks_and_Lupin_preparing_for_battle.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Tonks_and_Lupin_preparing_for_battle.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20110511111040" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tonks_and_Lupin_preparing_for_battle.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus and Tonks during the beginning stage of the final battle</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus was one of the many Order members who answered <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>'s call to arms on the 1st May, 1998. Harry, Hermione and Ron returned to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> gathered his army to attack the school in order to capture Harry Potter. He organised and led groups to fight <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> on the school grounds, along with <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a>. His wife initially agreed not to participate in the Battle of Hogwarts, instead staying with their infant son, but was ultimately unable to bear leaving her husband to face such danger without her.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a0/Remus_Lupin_%26_Nymphadora_Tonks_Deceased.png/revision/latest?cb=20170917233457" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="115" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus Lupin &amp; Nymphadora Tonks Deceased.png" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_&amp;_Nymphadora_Tonks_Deceased.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a0/Remus_Lupin_%26_Nymphadora_Tonks_Deceased.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170917233457" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a0/Remus_Lupin_%26_Nymphadora_Tonks_Deceased.png/revision/latest?cb=20170917233457" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a0/Remus_Lupin_%26_Nymphadora_Tonks_Deceased.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170917233457" decoding="async" width="245" height="115" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus Lupin &amp; Nymphadora Tonks Deceased.png" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_&amp;_Nymphadora_Tonks_Deceased.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a0/Remus_Lupin_%26_Nymphadora_Tonks_Deceased.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170917233457" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_Lupin_%26_Nymphadora_Tonks_Deceased.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The bodies of a deceased Remus and Tonks in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>She left Teddy with <a href="/wiki/Andromeda_Tonks" title="Andromeda Tonks">her mother</a> and raced to Hogwarts, where she was informed that Remus was last seen duelling Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Dolohov murdered Remus, who was no longer in prime fighting condition, due to months of protective and concealment charms in order to keep his wife and son safe from possible attacks. He was murdered in the Main Courtyard during the first half of the battle along with many others, including Tonks, his wife, who was murdered by her aunt <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Lupin's death was avenged by <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> who defeated or possibly murdered Dolohov.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-mortem">Post-mortem</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Post-mortem">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Post-mortem"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>I am sorry too... Sorry I will never know him... but he will know why I died and I hope he will understand.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin's parting words to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>During the brief pause in the battle, Remus and Tonks' bodies were laid out beside each other in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>. The nature of Remus' death was not revealed, but his body was described as peaceful-looking,<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> implying that he was struck with either a <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a> or <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov%27s_Curse" class="mw-redirect" title="Antonin Dolohov&#39;s Curse">Dolohov's own curse</a>; both are known to leave no visible marks on the outer body.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Harry-potter7-harry_lupin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170731055605" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-harry lupin.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-harry_lupin.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Harry-potter7-harry_lupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170731055605" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Harry-potter7-harry_lupin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170731055605" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Harry-potter7-harry_lupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170731055605" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-harry lupin.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-harry_lupin.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Harry-potter7-harry_lupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170731055605" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter7-harry_lupin.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A resurrected Remus talking with Harry in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, Remus still had an important part to play in the war. When Harry proceeded to the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> camp to be struck down by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, he first activated the Resurrection Stone, bringing back the spirits of his parents, Sirius, and Remus; Remus expressed the hope that Harry would care for his son, lamenting that he would never know him, but also found comfort in the fact that his son would know and understand why he died: he was trying to make a world in which his son could live a happier life.
</p><p>Remus Lupin was posthumously awarded the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">Order of Merlin</a>, First Class, the first werewolf ever to have been accorded this honour. The example of his life and death played an important role in lifting the stigma on werewolves among the wizarding society.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Physical appearance"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>The stranger was wearing an extremely shabby set of wizard's robes that had been darned in several places. He looked ill and exhausted. Though quite young, his light brown hair was flecked with grey.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Description of Lupin's outward appearance<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 146px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Remus_Lupin_profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100623122237" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="144" height="237" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus Lupin profile.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Remus_Lupin_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/144?cb=20100623122237" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Remus_Lupin_profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100623122237" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Remus_Lupin_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/144?cb=20100623122237" decoding="async" width="144" height="237" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus Lupin profile.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Remus_Lupin_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/144?cb=20100623122237" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_Lupin_profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus Lupin, age 36</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus was described as having a pale face with premature lines, and light brown hair that, as he progressed through his thirties, became more and more grey. The lines on his face and his greying hair were the results of the great deal of stress his body underwent with each full moon. His clothing is consistently shabby and patched, presumably because of his inability to find a decently-paid job due to his status as a werewolf.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, he sported a thin moustache, and from <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> until his death, he sported more of a rough beard. He had scars cutting across his face and given Remus' comments on werewolf inflicted injuries being cursed wounds that are unlikely to fully heal after <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>'s attack on <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a>, it is possible he had more scars from his self-inflicted injuries during his transformations. In death, however, the flaws of his appearance were rectified, just like his friend <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>; his spirit was described as "<i>younger, less shabby, and his hair was thicker and darker</i>."
</p><p>He was also quite tall, standing six feet, two inches tall. His height was not often mentioned, but is notable as his height corresponded roughly to the full length of a wolf's body from nose to tail. His 162 pound weight also corresponded to his wolfish dimensions. 
</p><p>In his werewolf form, he was a large beast with grey fur, and the only differences between his appearance and that of a true wolf being his shorter snout, more human eyes, and tufted tail. 
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>None of us is hiding Sirius Black under our cloaks. Go.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin bravely confronting a Dementor on the Hogwarts Express<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Remus was compassionate, intelligent, tolerant, levelheaded, peaceful, selfless, brave, kind, and good-natured. Despite having suffered a great deal of prejudice in his life due to his <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">lycanthropy</a>, he managed to retain an ability to see the good in almost everybody and was extremely forgiving. Remus also had an excellent sense of humour. When he was a student at school he was also part of the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> However, unlike his friends, he never partook in bullying. He hence could be described as the most mature and responsible one of the group. He even became a <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> in his fifth year.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Also he was able to, or at least would try to maintain civil conversation with those he did not get along well with.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Lupin1.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140705164156" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lupin1.gif" data-image-key="Lupin1.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Lupin1.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140705164156" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Lupin1.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140705164156" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Lupin1.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140705164156" decoding="async" width="245" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lupin1.gif" data-image-key="Lupin1.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Lupin1.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140705164156" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lupin1.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus demonstrating his flair for the subject he teaches by adding the element of music to a lesson</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> 
<p>Remus was unusually perceptive, with an uncanny ability to guess the thoughts of those around him. This is especially clear in his conversations with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, such as his intuiting that Harry was afraid that he thought he couldn't handle working with the <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">boggart</a>. He was a gifted teacher, with a rare flair for his subject and a profound understanding of his pupils. He was, as ever, drawn to the underdog, and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> especially benefited from his wisdom and encouragement. His perceptive nature is a rather ironic trait, given that wolves are rather intuitive and astute judges of character and communicate primarily through body language, a skill that Remus was extremely developed and talented at.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">"<i>There are worse things to lose than control.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin reciprocating the altruism and compassion shown by Chiara Lobasca<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Remus-lupin.png/revision/latest?cb=20060702225629" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="94" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus-lupin.png" data-image-key="Remus-lupin.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Remus-lupin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20060702225629" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Remus-lupin.png/revision/latest?cb=20060702225629" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Remus-lupin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20060702225629" decoding="async" width="240" height="94" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus-lupin.png" data-image-key="Remus-lupin.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Remus-lupin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20060702225629" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus-lupin.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus standing anxiously in the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>True to being a <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a>, Lupin was quite courageous. Nonetheless, he suffered deep-seated feelings of shame and fear of rejection which, in certain situations, led him to consider backing down. His greatest weakness was that, in his desperate longing to belong and be liked, he was neither as brave or honest as he should have been at times. Remus once claimed that he was cowardly, because he was unable to bring himself to tell <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> that <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> were <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagi</a>, as it would have meant that he had betrayed Dumbledore's trust, which meant everything to him. His love for James and Sirius also led him to not do anything to stop their bullying other students, a most notable example being when Snape was constantly bullied by his friends, but Remus was terrified of losing them and therefore did nothing to stop the bullying, something that he later admits to regret. Perhaps the most critical example of this was his temptation to join Harry, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> on Dumbledore's mission and abandon his wife and unborn son because he was afraid that her family would be ashamed of him being a werewolf. However, ultimately he came to his senses.
</p><p>He also was known to dislike the form of his <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> as it took the shape of a wolf. Lupin was disgusted by all things wolfish as they reminded him of his condition, and due to this has been known to deliberately cast a non-corporeal Patronus, particularly when in the company of others, for fear it would give him away as a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a>. The irony of this is that his desires to belong and be liked are that wolves are social animals, and often act in the interests of their pack, much like Remus' self-sacrificing nature, making him rather wolf-like even in his human form. In many ways, he represented the best parts of wolves, including his intelligence, adaptability, nurturing instincts, and his fierce desire to protect his loved ones.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Lupin%27s_boggart.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402100337" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="243" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lupin&#39;s boggart.gif" data-image-key="Lupin&#39;s_boggart.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Lupin%27s_boggart.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20190402100337" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Lupin%27s_boggart.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402100337" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Lupin%27s_boggart.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20190402100337" decoding="async" width="243" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lupin&#39;s boggart.gif" data-image-key="Lupin&#39;s_boggart.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Lupin%27s_boggart.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20190402100337" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lupin%27s_boggart.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus' very fitting boggart form</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>His <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a> was a full <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">moon</a>, reflecting on his terror of transforming into his <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> form near <a href="/wiki/Human" title="Human">humans</a>. It also showed his immense hatred and shame over his <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">condition</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA7_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA7-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Remus' nurturing instincts were incredibly wolfish. Due to his position being that of a moderator, teacher, and nurturer, Remus fit the wolf pack position of the "nanny" or sergeant, looking after and teaching younger wolves - in this case his students and younger Order members, and keeping his friends in line, albeit with limited success at times.
</p><p>In contrast to Sirius' more competitive and combative nature, Remus was far more peaceful, reserved, and prone to negotiation despite his nature as a werewolf. This is symbolic of how dogs often tend to fight for dominance versus the more pragmatic and somewhat democratic nature of wolves in a pack who organise themselves peacefully unless threatened. However, Remus was by no means weak and marched into battle against Voldemort's soldiers like a true warrior. Remus referred to Voldemort by name, unafraid of the Dark Lord or his loyal Death Eaters.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Lupin_Harry_wedding_DH_part1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151201015352" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="243" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lupin Harry wedding DH part1.jpg" data-image-key="Lupin_Harry_wedding_DH_part1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Lupin_Harry_wedding_DH_part1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20151201015352" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Lupin_Harry_wedding_DH_part1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151201015352" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Lupin_Harry_wedding_DH_part1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20151201015352" decoding="async" width="243" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lupin Harry wedding DH part1.jpg" data-image-key="Lupin_Harry_wedding_DH_part1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Lupin_Harry_wedding_DH_part1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20151201015352" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lupin_Harry_wedding_DH_part1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus at Bill and Fleur's Wedding talking to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After losing James, Sirius and Lily and all hope of reconciliation with Pettigrew gone, Remus had every reason to succumb to depression and despondency. However, he retained his appreciation for the good people existing in his life and continued to draw strength from them. 
</p><p>Lupin also must have been likely sceptical about <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a>, as <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Professor Trelawney</a> stated the he positively fled when she offered to <a href="/wiki/Crystal-gazing" title="Crystal-gazing">crystal gaze</a> him<sup id="cite_ref-POA11_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA11-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> (on another hand he could be merely afraid of what kind of things she could see, as his <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">lycanthropy</a>). 
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>You're the best Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher we've ever had!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> regarding Remus' skills<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Remus Lupin was an accomplished and skilful wizard, with extensive knowledge of <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark creatures</a>. He also possessed the ability to properly impart practical and theoretical skills of defensive magic to others. Remus was capable of conjuring a corporeal wolf Patronus (a mark of superior magical ability).<sup id="cite_ref-PM1_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM1-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> He also proved to be a skilful duellist, surviving numerous battles. However, by his own admission, <a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potions</a> was not his strong suit.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/LupinRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402100414" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="243" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="LupinRiddikulus.gif" data-image-key="LupinRiddikulus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/LupinRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20190402100414" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/LupinRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402100414" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/LupinRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20190402100414" decoding="async" width="243" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="LupinRiddikulus.gif" data-image-key="LupinRiddikulus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/LupinRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20190402100414" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:LupinRiddikulus.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lupin repelling his boggart with <i>Riddikulus</i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: In <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, Remus took the position of Defence Against the Dark Arts Professor at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>: Considered by most of his pupils to be the best teacher they had had in the subject, he was very knowledgeable on the subject of Dark <a href="/wiki/Creature" title="Creature">creatures</a> and how to handle them, as shown how he expertly taught this to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and his classmates during their third year. During his classes, he taught students about <a href="/wiki/Red_Cap" title="Red Cap">Red Caps</a>, <a href="/wiki/Grindylow" title="Grindylow">Grindylows</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kappa" title="Kappa">Kappas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vampire" title="Vampire">Vampires</a>, <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">Werewolves</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nocturnal_beasts" title="Nocturnal beasts">Nocturnal beasts</a> and <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggarts</a> (and how to repel them using the <a href="/wiki/Boggart-Banishing_Spell" title="Boggart-Banishing Spell">Boggart-Banishing Spell</a>), showing him to have had excellent knowledge of such fiendish creatures and the necessary defence against them. Known to have displayed a rare flair for his own subject, he would also have been very proficient on the subject of <a href="/wiki/Counter-curse" title="Counter-curse">counter-curses</a> and defensive spell-work, and, being a very proficient duellist, might very well have helped some of his older students become accomplished in combative magic themselves. He also taught Harry Potter the highly advanced <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a> to defend himself against <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> which he himself must have mastered at a relatively young age, at least when he joined the first <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. Remus' Patronus took the form of a <a href="/wiki/Wolf" title="Wolf">wolf</a>, a reflection of his condition, but he could disguise it into a non-corporeal form to hide that fact.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>There was a soft, crackling noise, and a shivering light filled the compartment. Professor Lupin appeared to be holding a handful of flames.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin using a nonverbal flame spell<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Wandless_magic" title="Wandless magic">Wandless</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">non-verbal magic</a></b>: While on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, Remus conjured fire (possibly <a href="/wiki/Bluebell_Flames" title="Bluebell Flames">Bluebell Flames</a>) <a href="/wiki/Wandless_magic" title="Wandless magic">without using a wand</a> and non-verbally.<sup id="cite_ref-POA5_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA5-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> He could also <a href="/wiki/Unlocking_Charm" title="Unlocking Charm">open</a> locks and chests and <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">relight candles</a> with just the wave of his hand. When Remus and Harry had a heated argument in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Remus struck him with a silent <a href="/wiki/Knockback_Jinx" title="Knockback Jinx">Knockback Jinx</a> so quickly that Harry barely had time to reach for <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_wand" title="Harry Potter&#39;s wand">his own</a> <a href="/wiki/Wand" title="Wand">wand</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> These were a testament to Remus being a truly powerful wizard, as both wandless and non-verbal magic are very difficult.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Remus_lupin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130731135557" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus lupin.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_lupin.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Remus_lupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130731135557" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Remus_lupin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130731135557" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Remus_lupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130731135557" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus lupin.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_lupin.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Remus_lupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130731135557" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_lupin.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lupin with his wand at the ready</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: Remus was a highly talented duellist. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, he was the only fighter besides <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and his pupil, Harry, who was not wounded, killed, or incapacitated. He was seen duelling <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> (the leader of the Death Eaters) in order to defend Harry and Neville from him and was able to emerge unscathed.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_14-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> He also came out of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a><sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> unscathed, and later survived the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a> despite his having to support an injured <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a> while fighting and flying during the conflict. Remus was also willing to personally fight the exceptionally skilled <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> after the latter injured George Weasley, though he opted instead to get himself and George to safety. Remus was ultimately killed in a duel during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> with <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>, a highly skilled and dangerous <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>, who had previously defeated extremely talented wizards such as <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> and the Prewett brothers, though chances were that he had put up an excellent fight; this downfall was due to Remus' months of staying at home with his wife under various <a href="/wiki/Protective_enchantment" title="Protective enchantment">protective enchantments</a>, the inactivity dulling his reflexes enough to weaken him for Dolohov to finally kill him.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/POA_Remus_Hogwarts_Express_against_Dementor.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190227201521" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="243" height="97" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="POA Remus Hogwarts Express against Dementor.gif" data-image-key="POA_Remus_Hogwarts_Express_against_Dementor.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/POA_Remus_Hogwarts_Express_against_Dementor.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20190227201521" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/POA_Remus_Hogwarts_Express_against_Dementor.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190227201521" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/POA_Remus_Hogwarts_Express_against_Dementor.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20190227201521" decoding="async" width="243" height="97" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="POA Remus Hogwarts Express against Dementor.gif" data-image-key="POA_Remus_Hogwarts_Express_against_Dementor.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/POA_Remus_Hogwarts_Express_against_Dementor.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20190227201521" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:POA_Remus_Hogwarts_Express_against_Dementor.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lupin conjuring a non-corporeal Patronus</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>So Lupin muttered something, and a silvery thing shot out of his wand at it, and it turned around and sort of glided away...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin's use of the Patronus Charm on a <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementor</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Remus was shown to have been talented in charms from a young age: as teenagers, he and his fellow Marauders (<a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter</a>) managed to create the magically complex <a href="/wiki/Marauder%27s_Map" title="Marauder&#39;s Map">Marauder's Map</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Homonculous_Charm" title="Homonculous Charm">Homonculous Charm</a>, the magic of which endured even long after the deaths of all four Marauders.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He was also able to cast a corporeal <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> (form of a <a href="/wiki/Wolf" title="Wolf">wolf</a>), which is regarded as a very advanced piece of <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a> as well as a sign of superior magical ability. The fact that he was even able to decide whether he wanted his Patronus to be corporeal or not was also a testament to his extraordinary talent in charms.<sup id="cite_ref-PM2_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM2-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> He was capable of casting numerous other enchantments, such as the <a href="/wiki/Boggart-Banishing_Spell" title="Boggart-Banishing Spell">Boggart-Banishing Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Seize_and_Pull_Charm" title="Seize and Pull Charm">Seize and Pull Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pack_Charm" title="Pack Charm">Pack Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Freezing_Spell" title="Freezing Spell">Freezing Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Freezing_Charm" title="Freezing Charm">Freezing Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/General_Counter-Spell" title="General Counter-Spell">General Counter-Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bandaging_Charm" title="Bandaging Charm">Bandaging Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/Waddiwasi" title="Waddiwasi">Waddiwasi</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Mobilicorpus" title="Mobilicorpus">Mobilicorpus</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Knockback_Jinx" title="Knockback Jinx">Knockback Jinx</a>, <a href="/wiki/Water-heating_spell" title="Water-heating spell">Water-heating spell</a> and even producing <a href="/wiki/Hand-held_flames" title="Hand-held flames">Hand-held flames</a>, for example.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i><a href="/wiki/Bandaging_Charm" title="Bandaging Charm">Ferula</a>." Bandages spun up Ron's leg, strapping it tightly to a splint. </i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Remus bandaging <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>'s leg<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Healing_magic" title="Healing magic">Healing magic</a></b>: In the spring of <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, Remus effectively used the <a href="/wiki/Bandaging_Charm" title="Bandaging Charm">Bandaging Charm</a> to bandage and splint broken bones on Ron, whose leg had been broken, showing him to have been skilled in the art of medical magic and with the casting of <a href="/wiki/Healing_spell" title="Healing spell">healing spells</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/88/Animagusreversalspell.png/revision/latest?cb=20130801124459" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="243" height="137" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Animagusreversalspell.png" data-image-key="Animagusreversalspell.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/88/Animagusreversalspell.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20130801124459" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/88/Animagusreversalspell.png/revision/latest?cb=20130801124459" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/88/Animagusreversalspell.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20130801124459" decoding="async" width="243" height="137" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Animagusreversalspell.png" data-image-key="Animagusreversalspell.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/88/Animagusreversalspell.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20130801124459" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Animagusreversalspell.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus and Sirius performing the <a href="/wiki/Animagus_reversal_spell" title="Animagus reversal spell">Animagus reversal spell</a> on Pettigrew</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Remus, along with Sirius, was able to perform <a href="/wiki/Untransfiguration" title="Untransfiguration">Untransfiguration</a> to force Peter to change into his human form (Peter's <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> form was a <a href="/wiki/Rat" title="Rat">rat</a>). He was also able to perform <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">conjuration</a>, which is an incredibly advanced form of Transfiguration: in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, he once <a href="/wiki/Incarcerous_Spell" title="Incarcerous Spell">conjured chains</a> to bind Peter to Ron. This shows he was highly proficient in this notably very difficult and complicated branch of <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">Flying</a></b>: Remus was chosen to lead the <a href="/wiki/Advance_Guard" title="Advance Guard">Advance Guard</a> when they escorted Harry from <a href="/wiki/4_Privet_Drive" title="4 Privet Drive">4 Privet Drive</a> in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_14-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> and he was able to evade and duel <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> while supporting an injured <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparition</a></b>: Being an accomplished wizard, Remus was capable of Apparating successfully. In <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, he Apparated to <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> to escape the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> from reaching him, allowing him to escape potential capture.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> (possibly)</b>: Remus was described as having “an odd, closed expression” right before he lied to <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, a skilled <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimens</a>. During his stay at Grimmauld Place, he was able to communicate with Sirius Black (also a possible Occlumens) while the two maintained eye contact for a lengthy period of time.</li>
<li><b>Teaching skills</b>: Despite his lack of previous teaching experience and poor lifestyle, Remus nevertheless proved to be a very skilled and talented teacher when he was briefly the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. This was because his lessons were more practical rather than theoretical and he had a profound understanding of his students, which motivated even <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> to improve. He was an enthusiastic teacher, inspiring students to take part and was very fair. Unlike the two teachers before him, he actually had a desire to teach students. As a result of his effective teaching methods, almost everyone (except some of the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> students) regarded him as the best Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher ever in the school despite his poor and shabby appearance and the revelation that he was a werewolf. His teaching skills were also effective enough to keep the Slytherin students and other wrongdoers under control even though they were critical of his poor and shabby appearance.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Indomitable willpower</b>: Lupin, in spite of his <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">Lycanthropy</a> and the life struggles he suffered as a result of it, was shown to have an incredibly strong willpower. During his school years, he was the only one among the four <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a> who did not participate in bullying <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> and other people even though he regretted not taking enough action to stop his other three friends from bullying them. Despite losing his three best friends when <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> suffered his first defeat when attempting to murder <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and being forced to live a lifestyle of poverty for 13 years as a result, Lupin never lost his appreciation for the good people still existing in his life which allowed him to accept <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>'s offer for him to teach <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Additionally, in spite of <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a>'s death at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, Lupin still retained enough emotional strength to restrain Harry from running through the <a href="/wiki/Veil" title="Veil">veil</a> after Sirius's body, check if Harry's friends were safe and unlike Harry, avoid pursuing revenge on Bellatrix even though the devastation of losing his last surviving Marauder friend was great for him. As he still drew strength from the good people in his life, this allowed him to keep fighting for the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> against Voldemort and his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, with Lupin notably never being afraid of uttering the Dark Lord's name aloud. When <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>'s ear was accidentally cursed off by Severus Snape, Lupin managed to carry George to safety even though he wished to have paid Snape back in kind, showing that his concern for others was greater than his longtime feud with Snape. Even though he was tempted to abandon his wife <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora</a> and <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">their unborn child</a> out of fear of passing his Lycanthropy to their son, he returned to his senses after a row with Harry and spent the rest of the war and his life protecting them and the other people he cared about. The level of willpower and courage Lupin displayed throughout his life to keep fighting for what was good despite having every reason to succumb to depression was what resulted in him being posthumously awarded the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">Order of Merlin</a> First Class, being the first <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> in history to receive that honour.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Possessions">Possessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Possessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Possessions"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 169px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Remus_wand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141208233259" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="167" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus wand.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_wand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Remus_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/167?cb=20141208233259" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Remus_wand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141208233259" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Remus_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/167?cb=20141208233259" decoding="async" width="167" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus wand.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_wand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Remus_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/167?cb=20141208233259" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_wand.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus' wand-10 and 1/4, cypress, contains unicorn hair core</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin%27s_wand" title="Remus Lupin&#39;s wand">Wand</a></b>: Like the vast majority of witches and wizards, it could be said that Remus' <a href="/wiki/Wand" title="Wand">wand</a> was most likely purchased at the age of eleven from <a href="/wiki/Ollivander%27s_Wand_Shop" class="mw-redirect" title="Ollivander&#39;s Wand Shop">Ollivanders</a>, and was counted among his most valued possessions. His wand was 10¼", <a href="/wiki/Cypress" title="Cypress">Cypress</a> <a href="/wiki/Wand_wood" title="Wand wood">wood</a>, and with <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_hair" title="Unicorn hair">unicorn hair</a> <a href="/wiki/Wand_core" title="Wand core">core</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin%27s_cottage" title="Remus Lupin&#39;s cottage">Cottage</a></b>: In <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, Remus lived alone in a cottage in Yorkshire, England. Albus Dumbledore tracked him to this cottage and offered him the post of Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher at Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin%27s_walking_stick" title="Remus Lupin&#39;s walking stick">Walking stick</a></b>: Remus used a walking stick after 1993 to facilitate his weakened state, induced by <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">lycanthropy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POAF_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POAF-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The extent of Remus' relationship with his family is unknown, aside from how adored he was by his parents. During Remus' youth, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin%27s_father" class="mw-redirect" title="Remus Lupin&#39;s father">his father</a> offended Fenrir Greyback, causing Greyback to attack Remus, when he was merely four years old. <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin%27s_father" class="mw-redirect" title="Remus Lupin&#39;s father">Mr</a> and <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin%27s_mother" class="mw-redirect" title="Remus Lupin&#39;s mother">Mrs Lupin</a> are known to have been concerned over Remus being a werewolf, believing that this condition meant their son would be unable to attend <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. However, this was proven untrue.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nymphadora_Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Nymphadora Tonks">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Nymphadora Tonks"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Nymphadora Tonks</b>: "<i>I don't care either, I don't care! I've told you a million times </i>[...]<i>  </i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Remus</b>: "<i>And I've told </i>you<i> a million times, that I am too old for you, too poor....too dangerous....</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Molly Weasley</b>: "<i>I've said all along you're taking a ridiculous line on this, Remus.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Remus</b>: "<i>I am not being ridiculous. Tonks deserves somebody young and whole.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Arthur Weasley</b>: "<i>But she wants </i>you<i>. And after all, Remus, young and whole men do not necessarily remain so.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Tonks, Arthur, and Molly try to convince Remus to be with Tonks<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222048" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nymphadora Tonks DH promo headshot .jpg" data-image-key="Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119222048" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222048" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119222048" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nymphadora Tonks DH promo headshot .jpg" data-image-key="Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119222048" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, his wife and mother of his son</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus and Tonks came to know each other as members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>. Remus, so often melancholy and lonely, was first amused, then impressed, then seriously smitten by the witch. He had never fallen in love before. If it had happened in peacetime, Remus would have simply taken himself off to a new place and a new job, so that he did not have to endure the pain of watching Tonks fall in love with a handsome, young wizard in the <a href="/wiki/Auror_Office" title="Auror Office">Auror Office</a> (which was what he expected to happen). However, this was war; they were both needed in the Order of the Phoenix, and nobody knew what the next day would bring. Remus felt justified in remaining exactly where he was, keeping his feelings to himself but secretly rejoicing every time somebody paired him with Tonks on some overnight mission.
</p><p>It had never occurred to Remus that Tonks could return his feelings because he had become so used to considering himself unclean and unworthy. One night when they lay in hiding outside a known Death Eater’s house, after a year of increasingly warm friendship, Tonks made an idle remark about one of their fellow Order members (<i>"He’s still handsome, isn't he, even after Azkaban?</i>"). Before he could stop himself, Remus had replied bitterly that he supposed she had fallen for his old friend ("<i>He always got the women.</i>"). At this, Tonks replied: "<i>You’d know perfectly well who I’ve fallen for, if you weren’t too busy feeling sorry for yourself to notice.</i>"
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Tonks_Lupin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100427183306" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="241" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tonks Lupin.jpg" data-image-key="Tonks_Lupin.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Tonks_Lupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100427183306" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Tonks_Lupin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100427183306" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Tonks_Lupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100427183306" decoding="async" width="180" height="241" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tonks Lupin.jpg" data-image-key="Tonks_Lupin.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Tonks_Lupin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100427183306" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tonks_Lupin.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nymphadora Tonks with husband, Remus Lupin</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus’s immediate response was a happiness he had never experienced in his life, but this was extinguished almost at once by a sense of crushing duty. He had always known that he could not marry and run the risk of passing on his painful, shameful condition. Wiser than Remus, she was sure that he loved her, but that he was refusing to admit it out of mistaken nobility. However, he avoided working with her, barely talked to her, and started volunteering for the most dangerous missions.
