Tonks became desperately unhappy, convinced not only that the man she loved would never willingly spend time with her again, but also that he might walk to his death rather than admit his feelings.
</p><p>Inspired by <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>’s protestation of enduring love for <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a>, who had been savaged by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Greyback</a>, Tonks made a brave, public declaration of her feelings for Remus, who was forced to admit the strength of his love for her. In spite of continuing misgivings that he was acting selfishly, Remus married Tonks quietly in the north of Scotland, with witnesses taken from the local wizarding tavern. He continued to fear that the stigma attached to him would infect his wife and wished for no fanfare around their union. He swung constantly between elation that he was married to the woman of his dreams and terror of what he might have brought upon them both. When she became pregnant, Remus was not delighted by this, he was in fact scared that he might be passing his condition on to an innocent child. He even attempted to abandon his pregnant wife and unborn child, but was stopped by Harry Potter. Realising the importance of staying with his family above all else, he returned to Tonks, bitterly ashamed.
</p><p>Lupin and Tonks were both murdered in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> in May 1998, leaving their son behind in the care of his maternal grandmother, <a href="/wiki/Andromeda_Tonks" title="Andromeda Tonks">Andromeda Tonks</a>, and his godfather, Harry Potter. Teddy was raised by Andromeda, but would spend a great deal of time with the <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley</a> families growing up. Teddy was a <a href="/wiki/Metamorphmagus" title="Metamorphmagus">Metamorphmagus</a>, like his mother.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Teddy_Lupin">Teddy Lupin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Teddy Lupin">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Teddy Lupin"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Yes, yes, she's had the baby!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Remus joyfully announces the birth of his son<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Teddy_Lupin.png/revision/latest?cb=20160801025828" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="313" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Teddy Lupin.png" data-image-key="Teddy_Lupin.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Teddy_Lupin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160801025828" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Teddy_Lupin.png/revision/latest?cb=20160801025828" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Teddy_Lupin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160801025828" decoding="async" width="180" height="313" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Teddy Lupin.png" data-image-key="Teddy_Lupin.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Teddy_Lupin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160801025828" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Teddy_Lupin.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Teddy Lupin</a>, his son and only child</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus' son was born in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>. Remus and his wife named him Edward, Teddy for short, after her father <a href="/wiki/Edward_Tonks" title="Edward Tonks">Ted Tonks</a>. At one point, Remus nearly abandoned <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">his wife</a> and unborn son, mostly out of premature shame, guilt, and the fear that his <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">lycanthropy</a> would be passed on and that he'd made outcasts out of Nymphadora and their child. Rather than wanting to face his impending fatherhood, he intended to help <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> with their mission of destroying Voldemort's Horcruxes (though he was actually unaware of what their "mission" entailed). Harry was, however, upset with the development and got into a rather heated argument with Remus that ultimately convinced him that the best course of action would be to support his family. He returned to his wife shortly thereafter.
</p><p>Teddy was eventually born and despite his earlier fears and insecurities about being a father, Remus expressed joy at his son's birth and asked Harry to be Teddy's godfather. Sadly, Remus and his wife were murdered at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, leaving Teddy an orphan when he was between two weeks and one month old. When Remus appeared again through the <a href="/wiki/Resurrection_Stone" title="Resurrection Stone">Resurrection Stone</a>, he was rather devastated knowing that Teddy would have to grow up without either of his parents, but found some solace in knowing that Teddy would be living in a better world. Teddy was raised by his maternal grandmother, but he spent significant time with his <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">godfather</a>'s family and the Weasleys.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marauders">Marauders</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Marauders">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Marauders"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>For the first time ever, I had friends, three great friends... I was terrified they would desert me the moment they found out what I was. But of course, they, like you, Hermione, worked out the truth...and they didn't desert me at all. Instead, they did something for me that would make my transformations not only bearable, but the best times of my life. They became Animagi.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Remus regarding his friends<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080414050923" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="198" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marauders 1997.jpg" data-image-key="Marauders_1997.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080414050923" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080414050923" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080414050923" decoding="async" width="250" height="198" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marauders 1997.jpg" data-image-key="Marauders_1997.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080414050923" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marauders_1997.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus with his best friends; James Potter, Sirius Black, and Peter Pettigrew</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As a Hogwarts student, Remus became good friends with fellow <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindors</a> <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>. In their second year, Remus' friends figured out that he was a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a>; instead of shunning him, as many in the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a> would have, they learned how to become <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagi</a> by their fifth year to accompany Remus on his monthly transformations, preventing him from hurting himself.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Because he was grateful to his friends, Remus cut them a lot of slack<sup id="cite_ref-JKR_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKR-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>; despite being dismayed by their bullying of <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, he did not attempt to stop them. Though he was his house's <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a>, Remus had difficulty trying to curb his friends' mischievous behaviour.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_14-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> However, Remus was not without a mischief-making streak himself, contributing to the invention of the <a href="/wiki/Marauder%27s_Map" title="Marauder&#39;s Map">Marauder's Map</a>.
</p><p>At some point, after Remus and his friends had all become members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, Sirius came to distrust Remus, fearing he might be a spy; the reasons for this are unknown. Sirius' distrust ensured that Remus was unaware when James and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily</a> changed their <a href="/wiki/Secret-Keeper" class="mw-redirect" title="Secret-Keeper">Secret-Keeper</a> from Sirius to Peter, and thus he believed that Sirius had betrayed them when they were murdered by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>. The two reclaimed their friendship after Sirius <a href="/wiki/Azkaban_escapes#1993" title="Azkaban escapes">escaped</a> from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, and Remus learned the truth. They planned to kill their traitorous former friend Peter, but were stopped by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Remus and Sirius both became close to their late friend's son, and Remus was devastated when Sirius was killed in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_14-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The ending of the three Marauders who had stayed true to their friendship to the very end — James, Sirius, and Remus — was bittersweet: they all lost their lives to the two wizarding wars but were likely reunited in the afterlife.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severus_Snape">Severus Snape</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Severus Snape">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Severus Snape"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Remus Lupin</b>: "<i>It comes down to whether or not you trust Dumbledore's judgement. I do; therefore, I trust Severus.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>But Dumbledore can make mistakes. He says it himself. And you — do you honestly like Snape?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Remus Lupin</b>: "<i>I neither like nor dislike Severus... We shall never be bosom friends, perhaps; after all that happened between James and Sirius and Severus, there is too much bitterness there. But I do not forget that during the year I taught at Hogwarts, Severus made the Wolfsbane Potion for me every month, made it perfectly, so that I did not have to suffer as I usually do at the full moon... I must be grateful.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Remus and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> on the former's relationship with Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, his former classmate and colleague</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Severus Snape, a <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> student in Remus' year, shared a strong enmity with Remus' close friends <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, who outright bullied Snape on occasion. Although not friendly with Snape, Remus never behaved cruelly to him. It is possible that he may have subtly identified with or sympathised with the lonely, isolated Snape, seeing a reflection of himself and how he would have been treated if he hadn't found the protection of his friends. Later in life, he said that he deeply regretted not having done anything to stop the bullying.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_14-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point in their fifth year, Snape saw <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Madam Pomfrey</a> leading Remus to the passageway on the full moon; Sirius thought it would be entertaining to inform Snape of how to freeze the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Whomping_Willow" title="Hogwarts Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a>. Snape tried to do so, but was stopped by James before he could reach the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>, where Remus had transformed. <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> forbade Snape from revealing Remus' condition to anyone, and Snape deeply resented being put in James' debt and suspected that Remus might have been in on the dangerous prank.
</p><p>As adults, Remus and Snape were civil to one another, although barely so on the latter's part. Remus claimed that he neither liked nor disliked Snape; of course they would never be bosom friends, after all that happened in their school days, but he also never forgot that Snape dutifully made him the Wolfsbane Potion, and made it perfectly every time so that he would not have to suffer at the full moon as he usually did. (Also, Snape secretly saved Lupin's life in <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle over Little Whinging</a>). Snape, on the other hand, barely concealed his bitterness in their interactions. He was irked that Remus obtained the position of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a> at Hogwarts, which he had always wanted for himself. He suspected that Remus was helping Sirius get into the castle and tried to convince Dumbledore to stop trusting him. Snape also took to dropping hints that Remus was a werewolf to students, which was understood by at least one of them (<a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, who kept the discovery to herself). When Remus tried to inform Snape of Sirius' innocence, Snape refused to hear or believe any of it, and was determined to see Remus punished alongside Sirius. When Snape's old enemy escaped re-capture, Snape vindictively exposed Remus' werewolf status, which forced him to resign.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In spite of all this, Remus believed that Snape was loyal to the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, encouraging <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to trust him and to continue his <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> lessons. He was shocked and angered when Snape killed <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, who had been the one to assure other Order members that Snape was trustworthy. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, Snape was one of the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> who attacked Remus and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>, the latter disguised as Harry by way of <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>. Snape, secretly still loyal to the Order, attempted to save Lupin by aiming a <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> at a Death Eater who was poised to kill Lupin, but accidentally struck George, who lost an ear. Remus, furious, expressed a desire to have "<i>paid him back in kind</i>", but had to focus on getting himself and George to safety.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Unfortunately Remus died before it was revealed that Snape was actually on his side the entire time, and had killed Dumbledore on his orders.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lily_Evans">Lily Evans</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lily Evans">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Lily Evans"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">"<i>Your mother was there for me at a time when no one else was.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Remus tells Harry of Lily's kindness<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140712171247" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="246" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lily Potter1.jpg" data-image-key="Lily_Potter1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140712171247" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140712171247" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140712171247" decoding="async" width="180" height="246" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lily Potter1.jpg" data-image-key="Lily_Potter1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140712171247" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lily_Potter1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>, his friend and mother of Harry <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Potter</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus met Lily Evans while they were both attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. Lily was not on good terms with two of Remus' dearest friends, James and Sirius, but that did not mean she disliked Remus as well, given that he acted more mature and thoughtful than his friends, and did not participate in their bullying though he did nothing to stop them either. 
</p><p>After Hogwarts, Lily married <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>. Although Sirius was the best man, Remus probably attended their wedding, too, given his status as one of their dearest friends. They all became members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>, and fought in several battles together. When Pettigrew betrayed the Potters to Voldemort, resulting in the tragic deaths of James and Lily, Remus was devastated. Later on, he became close to Lily's son, Harry, both as a paternal figure and a mentor. After Lupin was murdered during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, they were two of the four spirits whom Harry summoned using the Resurrection Stone .
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Molly, you're not the only person at this table who cares about Harry.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Remus regarding his feelings toward Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>: former student, good friend, and godfather to his son</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus met Harry Potter, the son of his late friends <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a>, for the first time since he was an infant, in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a> when he saved Harry from <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> on the Hogwarts Express. Remus was the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> during Harry's third year, and quickly became his favourite professor. The two bonded very closely. Remus found Harry to be; intelligent, kind, and an excellent Seeker, and had strong empathy for the pain that he had experienced throughout his life. Seeing him as the devoted, informative, fair and supportive man he is, Harry admired and cared about Remus even after he found out that he was a werewolf.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>If I’m proud of anything I’ve done this year, it’s how much you’ve learned... Tell me about your Patronus.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin's immense pride in Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Remus also told Harry that the first time he saw him, he recognised him not by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_scars#The_lightning-bolt_scar" title="Harry Potter&#39;s scars">his scar</a>, but by his eyes, which so closely resembled Lily's; unlike his predecessors <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, Remus did not greet Harry in an awed manner at meeting a living legend, but in a friendly and casual manner. It is suggested that Remus' classes were how Harry discovered his remarkable talent for Defence Against the Dark Arts. He took Harry aside to teach him the <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a>, assisted him in avoiding trouble with <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a>, and returned the <a href="/wiki/Marauder%27s_Map" title="Marauder&#39;s Map">Marauder's Map</a> to him once he was no longer a professor.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The two met again in the summer of <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>. Remus was part of <a href="/wiki/Advance_Guard" title="Advance Guard">the group</a> of <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order</a> members who transported Harry from Privet Drive to <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a>. Throughout the years, Remus shared with Harry many stories about his parents and <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">godfather</a>. He comforted Harry over Sirius' death and also offered him advice on other occasions.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_14-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a4/POA_Remus_Boggart_reveal.gif/revision/latest?cb=20090624184719" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="POA Remus Boggart reveal.gif" data-image-key="POA_Remus_Boggart_reveal.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a4/POA_Remus_Boggart_reveal.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090624184719" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a4/POA_Remus_Boggart_reveal.gif/revision/latest?cb=20090624184719" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a4/POA_Remus_Boggart_reveal.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090624184719" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="POA Remus Boggart reveal.gif" data-image-key="POA_Remus_Boggart_reveal.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a4/POA_Remus_Boggart_reveal.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090624184719" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:POA_Remus_Boggart_reveal.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus Lupin protecting Harry Potter when Harry's <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">boggart</a> turns into a <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementor</a> in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Just — just to be clear. You want to leave Tonks at her parents' house and come away with us?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Remus</b>: "<i>She'll be perfectly safe there, they'll look after her. Harry, I'm sure James would have wanted me to stick with you.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Well. I'm not. I'm pretty sure my father would have wanted to know why you aren't sticking with your own kid, actually.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Harry and Remus first and only argument<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>The only real disagreement they ever had was when Harry rejected Remus' offer to accompany him and his friends on the quest for Horcruxes. Harry became angry and cutting; he told his former teacher that he was being selfish and irresponsible for leaving his wife and unborn child. Remus responded with uncharacteristic violence and stormed out of the house, taking refuge in a corner of the Leaky Cauldron, where he sat drinking and fuming. However, after a few hours' reflection, Remus was forced to accept that his former-pupil had just taught him a valuable lesson. James and Lily, Remus reflected, had stuck with Harry even unto their own deaths. His own parents had sacrificed their peace and security to keep the family together. When Remus' son <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Teddy Lupin</a> was born, he asked that Harry be the boy's godfather, and after Remus' death, Harry played a prominent role in Teddy's life. Remus was one of the spirits that came out of the <a href="/wiki/Resurrection_Stone" title="Resurrection Stone">Resurrection Stone</a> to speak to Harry as he walked to what he believed was his death, indicating the almost familial bond between Remus and Harry.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> This familial bond can be compared to wolf behaviour, as it is common in wolf packs for the pups to be looked after by all members of the pack, much like how Harry was looked after and tutored by his father's friends, who in a way were part of James' "pack". 
</p><p>In <i><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts_and_Where_to_Find_Them" title="Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them">Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them</a></i>, Harry wrote in the werewolf section "<i>aren't all bad</i>", showing that Remus being a werewolf did not bother him at all.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hermione_Granger_and_Ron_Weasley">Hermione Granger and Ron Weasley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger and Ron Weasley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger and Ron Weasley"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Harry! How could you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>You shouldn’t have said that stuff to Lupin.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and Ron after <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> yells at Remus for leaving <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">his wife</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>

decoding="async" width="180" height="242" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" data-image-key="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20191008170323" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, his former students</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione Granger and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> were among the students who were very impressed by Remus' teaching when he was professor of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> for their third year. Hermione deduced that Remus was a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> (which was the actual goal of Severus Snape when he taught a lesson about werevolves as Lupin's substitute) early in the year, but kept this discovery to herself, not even telling her best friends; this is likely because she disapproved of the prejudice against werewolves and knew exposing the truth would hurt Remus. Although Ron initially reacted with fear to the revelation that Remus was a werewolf, he continued to admire and like Remus. In turn, Remus was fond of Ron and Hermione, and was particularly impressed by the latter's cleverness.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_11-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Ron and Hermione were shown to be very trusting of Lupin; when he appeared at Grimmauld Place, they lowered their wands as soon as he declared his name, something he reproached them for, "<i>speaking as their former <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher</i>." Also, they both disapproved when Harry yelled at Remus for leaving <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">his wife</a> during her pregnancy, although they did not entirely disagree with Harry's reasoning.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_31-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Albus_Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>On a happier note, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">I</a> am pleased to welcome two new teachers to our ranks <a href="/wiki/1993-1994_school_year" class="mw-redirect" title="1993-1994 school year">this year</a>. Firstly, Professor Lupin who had kindly consented to fill the post of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore introduces Remus<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="244" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" decoding="async" width="180" height="244" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, his former employer and friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Albus Dumbledore was considered by many to be the greatest <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> of all time, and Remus Lupin was among his many admirers and staunch supporters. Dumbledore was Remus' Headmaster during his time at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Dumbledore accepted Remus into his school, despite knowing his being a werewolf, as he valued Remus' strength of character and ability, and disregarded the stigma associated with his condition; the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">headmaster</a> personally approached the Lupin family to invite Remus to school, knowing full well of the circumstances. In fact, it was Dumbledore who, by several special precautions, ensured that Remus' werewolf status was kept secret during his school years, effectively preventing him from being ostracised from his school mates. 
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>I sometimes felt guilty about betraying Dumbledore’s trust, of course... he had admitted me to Hogwarts when no other headmaster would have done so, and he had no idea I was breaking the rules he had set down for my own and others’ safety. He never knew I had led three fellow students into becoming Animagi illegally.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lupin's respect for Dumbledore<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> found out what Remus truly was due to a cruel prank played on him by <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a>, Dumbledore was the one who swore him to secrecy. On his part, Remus confessed that Dumbledore's trust and exceptional kindness towards him meant everything to him, given that the vast majority of the wizarding world shunned him because of the deep prejudice towards werewolves, and Remus felt guilty for betraying this kindness by allowing his three <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauder</a> friends illegally become <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagi</a> and roaming wild during their schooling years. Despite this, after learning of Sirius's innocence, Dumbledore forgave Remus for his supposed betrayal, understanding his Marauder friends only became Animagi to help Remus in his werewolf form and considered it an extraordinary achievement.
</p><p>Dumbledore was also the founder and leader of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, an organisation that Remus joined after graduating from school, and he was trusted with many important missions. Remus was given the position of Defence Against the Dark Arts Professor at Hogwarts during the 1993–1994 school year, during which time Dumbledore requested that Snape brew the <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a> for Remus monthly; this, along with providing Remus with a paid job when he was suffering in poverty due to his condition, made Remus respect Dumbledore even more. Remus and Dumbledore fought alongside one another during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, where they suffered a devastating loss: Sirius, one of their dearest friends, died at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. Remus told Harry Potter on several occasions that he trusted Snape because Dumbledore did so. In 1997, Remus was devastated by Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a> after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, and demonstrated his loyalty and faith to Dumbledore by fighting and where he was assassinated by Antonin Dolohov a very powerful wizard he was avenged by Professor Filius Flitwick, his former teacher. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weasley_family">Weasley family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Weasley family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Weasley family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3e/Weasley_family_studio_01.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110222043720" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley family studio 01.jpg" data-image-key="Weasley_family_studio_01.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3e/Weasley_family_studio_01.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110222043720" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3e/Weasley_family_studio_01.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110222043720" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3e/Weasley_family_studio_01.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110222043720" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley family studio 01.jpg" data-image-key="Weasley_family_studio_01.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3e/Weasley_family_studio_01.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110222043720" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_family_studio_01.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Remus was always friendly with the Weasley family. He knew <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> since the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>, and they became friends again after Dumbledore led the second <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. Arthur and Remus fought together at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, where the latter was paired with Arthur's son, <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a>. He saved George's life, as George would have fallen off his broomstick when he was cursed by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. Arthur later thanked him for taking care of his son.
</p><p>Remus also lived for some time with the Weasley family at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a>. There, Remus agreed with <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly</a> not to tell Harry much about the Order of the Phoenix and Voldemort's plans. However, when Sirius argued with Molly, Remus didn't take either side.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and Remus seemed to have been friends, as they fought together in several battles of the Second War; they were also the ones who attempted to find <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Mad-Eye</a>'s dead body after the Battle of the Seven Potters. After the war, Remus and Tonks' <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">son</a> seemed to have a romantic relationship with Bill and Fleur's <a href="/wiki/Victoire_Weasley" title="Victoire Weasley">daughter</a>.
</p><p>Fred and George Weasley were also friends of Lupin. They were Lupin's students during their fifth year at Hogwarts and they also fought together at the Battle of the Seven Potters. Remus protected George from being killed; however, George's ear was accidentally cut off by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. Lupin and the twins also appeared on the underground radio programme <i><a href="/wiki/Potterwatch" title="Potterwatch">Potterwatch</a></i> and spoke to the wizarding community during the last year of the war. Both Fred and Lupin were killed during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p><p>He was also friends with <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a>. He first met her at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>, saved her from the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> and gave her chocolate and comforted her, and she stated that he was one of her favourite professors at Hogwarts. They fought on the same side at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> and survived the battle. After the war, Ginny and the rest of the Potter family shared a close relationship with Teddy Lupin, who came to Ginny and Harry's house for dinner four times a week.
</p><p>His relationship with <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a> was almost unknown. When Lupin was Defence Against the Dark Arts professor, Percy most likely thought he was a good teacher. They met each other again during the Battle of Hogwarts, when Percy told his family that he had left the Ministry and wanted to join the Order, though there would hardly have been time for the two to become close.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_residents">Hogwarts residents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts residents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Hogwarts residents"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>Dumbledore hired you when he knew you were a werewolf. Is he mad?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Remus Lupin</b>: "<i>Some of the staff thought so. He had to work very hard to convince certain teachers that I’m trustworthy —</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; How Lupin gained acceptance as a Hogwarts teacher<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140521115100" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="253" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Minerva McGonagall POAF promo.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521115100" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140521115100" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521115100" decoding="async" width="180" height="253" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Minerva McGonagall POAF promo.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521115100" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, his former head of house and professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Lupin was a student at Hogwarts, the professors seemed to like him, especially Minerva McGonagall, who had been his head of house. His professors probably considered Lupin a skilled wizard and a very good student, as he was made a <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> in his fifth year.
</p><p>When Lupin became a professor, the other professors appeared to like and respect him, with the exception of <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. They either did not mind that he was a werewolf or did not show it, as they had been informed of his condition. Minerva even made reference to Lupin's evaluations on Harry's Defence Against the Dark Arts skills during a Careers Advice session. Many of them later fought alongside Remus at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p><p>Many of the students, including <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, and the Weasleys liked him. While others, such as <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> and several other <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherins</a>, disliked and regularly insulted him. Malfoy underestimated Lupin because of his poor-looking appearance. However, Lupin managed to be well-respected (and one of the best-liked professors), as he treated all the students based on their character, and not by their magical abilities, their blood status, or their wealth. When he left Hogwarts, many students continued to regard him as the best Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher they had.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Order_of_the_Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest?cb=20140511035621" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest?cb=20140511035621" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Remus had a good relationship with the most of the Order of the Phoenix. In addition to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, he was friends with many of members.
</p><p>One of his friends through the order was <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>. They fought together in several battles of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, and appeared to be close enough. They also appeared on <i><a href="/wiki/Potterwatch" title="Potterwatch">Potterwatch</a></i> together during the last year of the war.
</p><p>He was also a friend of <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>. They fought together in many battles, until Moody was killed by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>. Remus was devastated, as were many other members of the Order.
</p><p>Remus was one of the many members of the Order of the Phoenix murdered during Second Wizarding War.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 172px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Lupin%27swand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090512025509" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="170" height="170" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lupin&#39;swand.jpg" data-image-key="Lupin&#39;swand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Lupin%27swand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20090512025509" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Lupin%27swand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090512025509" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Lupin%27swand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20090512025509" decoding="async" width="170" height="170" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lupin&#39;swand.jpg" data-image-key="Lupin&#39;swand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Lupin%27swand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20090512025509" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lupin%27swand.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus Lupin</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>The name "Remus" comes from the brothers Romulus and Remus, the legendary brothers who fought to the death over the control of Rome, having been raised by a mother wolf whose cubs had died. Because of this, some fans speculated that Remus had a brother, but "Romulus" is merely the code name used by Lupin for <i><a href="/wiki/Potterwatch" title="Potterwatch">Potterwatch</a></i>. Remus' intense rivalry with Romulus indicates Lupin's ongoing struggle with his other side, the werewolf.</li>
<li>"Lupin" is derived from "lupinus", Latin for "wolf-like"; "lupus", or "wolf", being the basic word. <i>Canis l​upus</i> is the scientific name for the wolf - to be described as "lupine" means to "resemble a wolf." Lupin is also the name of an plant with edible seeds. The surname may also be derived from the character of Arsène Lupin, a fictional gentleman thief and master of disguise, who was created by French writer Maurice Leblanc in 1905. In Leblanc's novels, Arsène Lupin is often a force for good, while operating on the wrong side of the law. Leblanc's Lupin was said to have later inspired the character of "the Lone Wolf", a jewel thief-turned-private detective in a series of novels written by Louis Joseph Vance, beginning in 1914.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=38" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
