<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 142px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/YoungRemusLupinWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200718120723" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="140" height="436" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="YoungRemusLupinWU.png" data-image-key="YoungRemusLupinWU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/YoungRemusLupinWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/140?cb=20200718120723" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/YoungRemusLupinWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200718120723" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/YoungRemusLupinWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/140?cb=20200718120723" decoding="async" width="140" height="436" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="YoungRemusLupinWU.png" data-image-key="YoungRemusLupinWU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/YoungRemusLupinWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/140?cb=20200718120723" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:YoungRemusLupinWU.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Young Remus Lupin as he appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Wizards_Unite" title="Harry Potter: Wizards Unite">Harry Potter: Wizards Unite</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Remus Lupin being a werewolf could have been predicted merely by his name. Remus is from a roman story about two demigod/prince brothers, <b>Remus</b> and, the founder of Rome, Romulus, who were raised by a <b>wolf</b>. Lupin is a take on the Latin word for wolf, <i>lupus.</i></li>
<li>Remus Lupin is unique among the teachers as he calls students per their first names, not surnames. The only other teachers that are known to do this is the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">professor</a>.</li>
<li>Remus Lupin is the only <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauder</a> to be on anything resembling civil terms with <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> as adults. <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a> and Snape had often argued as adults. <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Pettigrew</a> was treated with contempt by Snape, going so far into being treated as a house servant at Snape's personal residence at <a href="/wiki/Spinner%27s_End" title="Spinner&#39;s End">Spinner's End</a>.</li>
<li>With his marriage to <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, Remus became related through his wife to the Malfoys, the Blacks, the Lestranges, the Weasleys, the Potters, the Longbottoms, and other pure-blood families.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>The Marauders write their names on the Marauder's Map in this order: Remus, Peter, Sirius and James. Ironically, this, when reversed, is the order in which they die, James being the first in <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>, <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a>; Sirius in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a>; Peter in <a href="/wiki/March" title="March">March</a> <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>; Remus in <a href="/wiki/May" title="May">May</a> <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>.
<ul><li>Remus survived the longest out of all the Marauders, beating Wormtail by some chapters in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>.</li></ul></li>
<li>After the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, 13 people (Mr and Mrs Weasley, Bill, Fleur, Fred, George, Ron, Ginny, Harry, Hermione, Remus, Tonks and Hagrid) gathered in <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">The Burrow</a> to mourn the death of <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>. Afterwards, Remus stood up and offered to look for Moody's dead body. Later in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Remus was killed by <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a> thus making another of <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Trelawney</a>'s predictions come true for the third time (first time on <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, and second on <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>)&#160;: that <i>when thirteen dine together, the first to rise will be the first to die</i>. However, as it is not known when Remus died, it is possible that Fred died before him.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> wrote a full-length biography of Remus for <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i> on  <i><a href="/wiki/Pottermore" title="Pottermore">Pottermore</a></i>, which was released in the final instalment of the book, and provided information on his and <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>'s relationship, as well as his youth.<sup id="cite_ref-IN_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IN-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Remus is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> actor <a href="/wiki/David_Thewlis" title="David Thewlis">David Thewlis</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)">film adaptations</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Half-Blood Prince</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Part 2</a></i>.
<ul><li>Thewlis had originally auditioned for the part of <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Professor Quirinus Quirrell</a>, but <a href="/wiki/Ian_Hart" title="Ian Hart">Ian Hart</a> was eventually cast.</li>
<li>David Thewlis has said that <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i> director <a href="/wiki/Alfonso_Cuar%C3%B3n" title="Alfonso Cuarón">Alfonso Cuaron</a> told him to portray Remus as a "gay junkie".<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>In the books, Remus plays a relatively large part in Harry's life after he left Hogwarts as Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher. However, in the films, Remus plays a large part in <i>Prisoner of Azkaban</i>, and then his role is drastically reduced. His argument and brief falling out with Harry in <i>Deathly Hallows</i> is cut out, as is his bitterness at being a father. The audience is not made aware of Remus' child until a throwaway line in <i>Deathly Hallows: Part 2</i>. <i>Half-Blood Prince</i> also cuts down his role, eliminating Remus' concerns about being in a relationship with Tonks.
<ul><li>David Thewlis was disappointed about his smaller appearances in the films, expressing a desire to be more involved.</li></ul></li>
<li>Originally, Remus and Nymphadora were supposed to survive the Battle of Hogwarts, but Rowling eventually killed them off as compensation after sparing <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> from the death, as he was originally intended to die in either the fifth book or the seventh book.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Trolley_witch" title="Trolley witch">witch who pushes the lunch trolley</a>, Remus, and <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> are the only adults ever to be seen travelling to Hogwarts on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">school train</a> in the book <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(book_series)" title="Harry Potter (book series)">series</a> (the latter is never shown on the train in the films). Though the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express_conductor" title="Hogwarts Express conductor">conductor</a> is never shown in the books, he is seen in some of the video game adaptations.</li>
<li>It was predicted by many fans that Wormtail would kill Remus with his silver hand, as Remus is a werewolf. However, J.K. Rowling mentioned in an interview that, contrary to what is seen in films, in her view werewolves are not affected by silver. Ironically the Marauder that does die by the silver hand is not Lupin, but Wormtail himself.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, Remus and Nymphadora were already in a relationship, rather then Remus initially rejecting her feelings since during the Christmas scene at <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">The Burrow</a> she calls him "sweetheart".</li>
<li>In an earlier draft of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> class may have been taught by a woman.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>His name is the inspiration for the <a href="/wiki/Wizard_rock" title="Wizard rock">wizard rock</a> bands <a href="/wiki/Remus_and_the_Lupins" title="Remus and the Lupins">Remus and the Lupins</a> and <a href="/wiki/The_Remus_Lupins" title="The Remus Lupins">The Remus Lupins</a>.</li>
<li>According to StarDate Online's Moon Phase Calculator, Remus' birth date (10 March, 1960), fell two days before a full moon.</li>
<li>Although Remus provides most of the books' information on the Patronus Charm, his own Patronus was never revealed in any of the books or media associated with the franchise until the release of the final chapters of <i>Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</i> on  <i><a href="/wiki/Pottermore" title="Pottermore">Pottermore</a></i>. His corporeal Patronus takes the form of a <a href="/wiki/Wolf" title="Wolf">wolf</a>, rather than a werewolf. Despite this, he normally preferred to purposely cast it as a non-corporeal form, as he considered the corporeal form to be too much of a giveaway.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>J. K. Rowling has indirectly stated that, if Remus Lupin were to take a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Myers%E2%80%93Briggs_Type_Indicator" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Myers–Briggs Type Indicator">Myers–Briggs Type Indicator</a> assessment, his personality type would be <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ENFJ" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ENFJ">ENFJ</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>The irony of his status as a werewolf and his desire to be liked and belong is that wolves are social animals that tend to live in packs and act in the interests of all, reflecting his selfless and self-sacrificing nature. This, combined with the typically savage side of his werewolf forms presents an almost yin-yang-like inner conflict, with his human form representing the better half of his wolfish personality, such as his intelligence, kindness, adaptability, and desire to defend. All the while his werewolf form represents the more savage aspects of wolves, such as feral wrath, gluttony, and lust.
<ul><li>Another bit of irony is in his love of chocolate, as it is poisonous to wolves and other canines.</li></ul></li>
<li>In the films Remus is shown to be a fan of jazz music, and owns an antique record player.</li>
<li>Remus' tendency to nurture those around him, particularly children, is fitting, as wolves' social structure commonly involves all members of the pack looking after and teaching the pups. Yet another instance where Remus lives up to the nobler aspects of his wolfish nature. Rather ironically, he considered himself unfit for parenthood.</li>
<li>Lupin was Harry's only Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher who was not antagonistic to him. (Not including when Lupin tried attacking him in his werewolf form).</li></ul>
<h3><span id="Author's_comments"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Author.27s_comments">Author's comments</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?veaction=edit&amp;section=39" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Author&#039;s comments">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Author&#039;s comments"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> has stated that Professor Lupin is the kind of teacher she wishes she had while she was a student. He is good-natured, kind, and able to extract the best in everyone — for example, in spotting <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>'s lack of confidence and helping him to overcome it by teaching him how to defeat the <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">boggart</a>.
</p><p>The fact that Remus is a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> and needs to take a <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">potion</a> to avoid hurting people for the rest of his life makes him a symbol of the consequences of prejudice and segregation, as well as society's often negative reaction to the ill and the disabled. Particularly, the author has stated that Remus Lupin's characterisation and history are H.I.V. metaphors (e.g. someone who was infected young and suffered prejudice because of it; terrified of passing the condition on), as well as an exploration into why someone might become embittered as a result of contracting such a condition.<sup id="cite_ref-legal_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-legal-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As such, Rowling has also stated that "Lupin's failing is he likes to be liked. That's where he slips up — he's been disliked so often he's always pleased to have friends so cuts them an awful lot of slack."<sup id="cite_ref-JKR_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKR-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> This is why, for instance, despite disapproving of his friends' bullying of <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, he once tried to stop them but failed and never tried again.
</p><p>Lupin was killed off in place of Arthur Weasley to remove the last of Harry's father figures in the books, and also to create a parallel between Harry's life and Teddy Lupin's. Rowling felt it was important to show the evils of Voldemort's actions and the devastating nature of war.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> She says she only decided to kill Remus at the end of the fifth book.
</p><p>Rowling has said that Remus is one of her favourite characters, and that if she could meet any of her characters, she would likely choose him.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
